    <text xml:lang="sa-Latn">

        <body>
            <div n="1" type="sthāna">

                <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 1-31]</head>

                <div n="1" type="adhyāya">



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāto vedotpattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||1|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ||2||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.3</label>
                        <caesura/> atha khalu bhagavantam amaravaram ṛṣigaṇaparivṛtam āśramasthaṃ
                        kāśirājaṃ divodāsaṃ dhanvantarim aupadhenava<pc
                            > </pc>vaitaraṇaurabhra<pc> </pc>pauṣkalāvata<pc
                            > </pc>-karavīrya<pc> </pc>gopurarakṣita<pc> </pc>suśruta<pc
                        > </pc>prabhṛtaya ūcuḥ ||3|| <note type="footnote"> karavīra</note>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.4</label>
                        <caesura/> bhagavan śārīramānasāgantuvyādhibhir
                        vividhavedanābhighātopadrutān sanāthān apy anāthavad viceṣṭamānān vikrośataś
                        ca mānavān abhisamīkṣya manasi naḥ pīḍā bhavati </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.4b">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.4b</label>
                        <caesura/> teṣāṃ sukhaiṣiṇāṃ rogopaśamārtham ātmanaś ca prāṇayātrārthaṃ
                        prajāhitahetor āyurvedaṃ śrotum icchāma ihopadiśyamānaṃ atrāyattam aihikam
                        āmuṣmikaṃ ca śreyaḥ tad bhagavantam upapannāḥ smaḥ śiṣyatveneti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.5</label>
                        <caesura/> tān uvāca bhagavān svāgataṃ vaḥ sarva evāmīmāṃsyā adhyāpyāś ca
                        bhavanto vatsāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.6</label>
                        <caesura/> iha khalv āyurvedaṃ nāmopāṅgam atharvavedasyānutpādyaiva prajāḥ
                        ślokaśatasahasram adhyāyasahasraṃ ca kṛtavān svayambhūḥ tato 'lpāyuṣṭvam
                        alpamedhastvaṃ cālokya narāṇāṃ bhūyo 'ṣṭadhā praṇītavān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.7</label>
                        <caesura/> tad yathā śalyaṃ śālākyaṃ kāyacikitsā bhūtavidyā kaumārabhṛtyaṃ
                        agadatantraṃ rasāyanatantraṃ vājīkaraṇatantram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāsya pratyaṅgalakṣaṇasamāsaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.1a">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.1a</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra śalyaṃ nāma
                        vividhatṛṇakāṣṭhapāṣāṇapāṃśulohaloṣṭāsthibālanakhapūyāsrāvaduṣṭavraṇāntargarbhaśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ
                        yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānavraṇaviniścayārthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.2</label>
                        <caesura/> śālākyaṃ nāmordhvajatrugatānāṃ
                        śravaṇanayanavadanaghrāṇādisaṃśritānāṃ vyādhīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.3</label>
                        <caesura/> kāyacikītsā nāma sarvāṅgasaṃśritānāṃ vyādhīnāṃ
                        jvararaktapittaśoṣonmādāpasmārakuṣṭhamehātisārādīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.4</label>
                        <caesura/> bhūtavidyā nāma
                        devāsuragandharvayakṣarakṣaḥpitṛpiśācanāgagrahādyupasṛṣṭacetasāṃ
                        śāntikarmabaloharaṇādigrahopaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.5</label>
                        <caesura/> kaumārabhṛtyaṃ nāma kumārabharaṇadhātrīkṣīradoṣasaṃśodhanārthaṃ
                        duṣṭastanyagrahasamutthānāṃ ca vyādhīnām upaśamanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.6</label>
                        <caesura/> agadatantraṃ nāma sarpakīṭalūtāmūśikādidaṣṭaviṣavyañjanārthaṃ
                        vividhaviṣasaṃyogopaśamanārthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.7</label>
                        <caesura/> rasāyanatantraṃ nāma vayaḥsthāpanam āyurmedhābalakaraṃ
                        rogāpaharaṇasamarthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.8.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.8.8</label>
                        <caesura/> vājīkaraṇatantraṃ nāmālpaduṣṭakṣīṇaviśuṣkaretasām
                        āpyāyanaprasādopacayajanananimittaṃ praharṣajananārthaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.9</label>
                        <caesura/> evam ayam āyurvedo 'ṣṭāṅga upadiśyate atra kasmai kim ucyatām iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.10</label>
                        <caesura/> ta ūcuḥ asmākaṃ sarveṣām eva śalyajñānaṃ mūlaṃ kṛtvopadiśatu
                        bhagavān iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.11</label>
                        <caesura/> sa uvācaivam astv iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.12</label>
                        <caesura/> ta ūcur bhūyo 'pi bhagavantam asmākam ekamatīnāṃ matam
                        abhisamīkṣya suśruto bhagavantaṃ prakṣyati asmai copadiśyamānaṃ vayam apy
                        upadhārayiṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.13</label>
                        <caesura/> sa hovācaivam astv iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.14-16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.14-16</label>
                        <caesura/> vatsa suśruta iha khalv āyurvedaprayojanaṃ vyādhyupasṛṣṭānāṃ
                        vyādhiparimokṣaḥ svasthasya rakṣaṇaṃ ca || āyur asmin vidyate 'nena vā+āyur
                        vindatīty āyurvedaḥ || tasyāṅgavaram ādyaṃ pratyakṣāgamānumānopamānair
                        aviruddham ucyamānam upadharaya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.17.adda">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.17.adda</label>
                        <caesura/> etad dhy aṅgaṃ prathamaṃ prāg abhighātavraṇasaṃrohāt
                        yajñaśiraḥsandhānāc ca | śrūyate hi yathā rudreṇa yajñasya śiraś chinnam iti </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.17b">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.17b</label>
                        <caesura/> tato devā aśvināv abhigamyocuḥ bhagavantau naḥ śreṣṭhatamau yuvāṃ
                        bhaviṣyathaḥ bhavadbhyāṃ yajñasya śiraḥ sandhātavyam iti | tāv ūcatur evam
                        astv iti | atha tayor arthe devā indraṃ yajñabhagena prāsādayan | tābhyāṃ
                        yajñasya śiraḥ saṃhitam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.18</label>
                        <caesura/> aṣṭāsv api cāyurvedatantreṣv etad evādhikam abhimataṃ āmāśu
                        kriyākaraṇād yantraśastrakṣārāgnipraṇidhānāt sarvatantrasāmānyāc ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.19</label>
                        <caesura/> tad idaṃ śāśvataṃ puṇyaṃ svargyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ vṛttikaraṃ ceti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.20</label>
                        <caesura/> brahmā provāca tataḥ prajāpatir adhijage tasmād aśvinau aśvibhyām
                        indraḥ indrād aḥaṃ mayā tv iha pradeyam arthibhyaḥ prajāhitahetoḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.21</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | ahaṃ hi dhanvantarir ādidevo jarārujāmṛtyuharo
                        'marāṇām | <caesura/> śalyāṅgam aṅgair aparair upetaṃ prāpto 'smi gāṃ bhūya
                        ihopadeṣṭum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.22</label>
                        <caesura/> asmin śāstre pañcamahābhūtaśarīrisamavāyaḥ puruṣa ity ucyate |
                        tasmin kriyā so 'dhiṣṭhānaṃ kasmāt lokasya dvaividhyāt loko hi dvividhaḥ
                        sthāvaro jaṅgamaś ca dvividhātmaka evāgneyaḥ saumyaś ca tadbhūyastvāt
                        pañcātmako vā tatra caturvidho bhūtagrāmaḥ
                        saṃsvedajarāyujāṇḍajodbhijjasaṃjñaḥ tatra puruṣaḥ pradhānaṃ tasyopakaraṇam
                        anyat tasmāt puruṣo 'dhiṣṭhānam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.23</label>
                        <caesura/> tad duḥkhasaṃyogā vyādhaya ucyante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.24</label>
                        <caesura/> te caturvidhāḥ āgantavaḥ śārīrāḥ mānasāḥ svābhāvikāś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.1</label>
                        <caesura/> teṣām āgantavo 'bhighātanimittāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.2</label>
                        <caesura/> śārīrās tv annapānamūlā
                        vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātavaiṣamyanimittāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.3</label>
                        <caesura/> mānasās tu
                        krodhaśokabhayaharṣaviṣāderṣyābhyasūyādainyamātsaryakāmalobhaprabhṛtaya
                        icchādveṣabhedair bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.25.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.25.4</label>
                        <caesura/> svābhāvikās tu kṣutpipāsājarāmṛtyunidrāprakṛtayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.26">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.26</label>
                        <caesura/> ta ete manaḥśarīrādhiṣṭhānāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.27</label>
                        <caesura/> teṣāṃ saṃśodhanasaṃśamanāhārācārāḥ samyak prayuktā nigrahahetavaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.28</label>
                        <caesura/> prāṇināṃ punar mūlam āhāro balavarṇaujasāṃ ca sa ṣaṭsu raseṣv
                        āyattaḥ rasāḥ punar dravyāśrayāḥ dravyāṇi punar oṣadhayaḥ | tās tu dvividhāḥ
                        sthāvarā jaṅgamāś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.29</label>
                        <caesura/> tāsāṃ sthāvarāś caturvidhāḥ vanaspatayo vṛkṣā vīrudha oṣadhaya
                        iti | tāsu apuṣpāḥ phalavanto vanaspatayaḥ puṣpaphalavanto vṛkṣāḥ
                        pratānavatyaḥ stambinyaś ca vīrudhaḥ phalapākaniṣṭhā oṣadhaya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.30</label>
                        <caesura/> jaṅgamāḥ khalv api caturvidhāḥ jarāyujāṇḍajasvedajodbhijjāḥ |
                        tatra paśumanuṣyavyālādayo jarāyujāḥ khagasarpasarīsṛpaprabhṛtayo 'ṇḍajāḥ
                            kṛmi<pc> </pc>kīṭa<pc> </pc>pipīlikā<pc> </pc>prabhṛtayaḥ svedajāḥ
                        indragopamaṇḍūkaprabhṛtaya udbhijjāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.31</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra sthāvarebhyas
                        tvakpatrapuṣpaphalamūlakandaniryāsasvarasādayaḥ prayojanavantaḥ jaṅgamebhyaś
                        carmanakharomarudhirādayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.32</label>
                        <caesura/> pārthivāḥ suvarṇarajatamaṇimuktāmanaḥśilāmṛtkapālādayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.33">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.33</label>
                        <caesura/> kālakṛtāḥ
                        pravātanivātātapacchāyājyotsnātamaḥśītoṣṇavarṣāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanādayaḥ
                        saṃvatsaraviśeṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.34">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.34</label>
                        <caesura/> ta ete svabhāvata eva doṣāṇāṃ
                        sañcayaprakopapraśamapratīkārahetavaḥ prayojanavantaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.35">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.35</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ <caesura/> śārīrāṇāṃ vikārāṇām eṣa vargaś
                        caturvidhaḥ | <caesura/> prakope praśame caiva hetur uktaś cikitsakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.36">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.36</label>
                        <caesura/> āgantavas tu ye rogās te dvidhā nipatanti hi | <caesura/> manasy
                        anye śarīre 'nye teṣāṃ tu dvividhā kriyā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.37</label>
                        <caesura/> śarīrapatitānāṃ tu śārīravad upakramaḥ | <caesura/> mānasānāṃ tu
                        śabdādir iṣṭo vargaḥ sukhāvahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.38">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.38</label>
                        <caesura/> evam etat puruṣo vyādhir auṣadhaṃ kriyā kāla iti catuṣṭayaṃ
                        samāsena vyākhyātam | tatra puruṣagrahaṇāt tatsaṃbhavadravyasamūho bhūtādir
                        uktas tadaṅgapratyaṅgavikalpāś ca tvaṅmāṃsāsthisirāsnāyuprabhṛtayaḥ
                        vyādhigrahaṇād vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātavaiṣamyanimittāḥ sarva eva
                        vyādhayo vyākhyātāḥ oṣadhagrahaṇād dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākānām ādeśaḥ
                        kriyāgrahaṇāc chedyādīni snehādīni ca karmāṇi vyākhyātāni kālagrahaṇāt
                        sarvakriyākālānām ādeśaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.39">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.39</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> bījaṃ cikitsitasyaitat samāsena
                        prakīrtitam | <caesura/> saviṃśam adhyāyaśatam asya vyākhyā bhaviṣyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.40">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.40</label>
                        <caesura/> tac ca saviṃśam adhyāyaśataṃ pañcasu sthāneṣu
                        sūtranidānaśārīracikitsitakalpeṣv arthavaśāt saṃvibhajya uttare tantre śeṣān
                        arthān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.41">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.1.41</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> svayambhuvā proktam idaṃ sanātanaṃ
                        <caesura/> paṭhed dhi yaḥ kāśipatiprakāśitam | <caesura/> sa puṇyakarmā
                        bhuvi pūjito nṛpair <caesura/> asukṣaye śakrasalokatāṃ vrajet || </l>




                    <p xml:id="SS.1.1">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne vedotpattir nāma prathamo
                        'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                </div>


                <div n="2" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ|]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaḥ śiṣyopanayanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.3</label>
                        <caesura/> brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyānām anyatamam anvaya<pc
                            > </pc>vayaḥ<pc/>śīla<pc> </pc>śaurya<pc> </pc>śaucācāra<pc
                            > </pc>vinaya<pc> </pc>śakti<pc> </pc>bala<pc> </pc>medhā<pc
                            > </pc>dhṛti<pc> </pc>smṛti<pc> </pc>mati<pc> </pc>pratipattiyuktaṃ
                            tanu<pc> </pc>jihvauṣṭha<pc> </pc>dantāgram ṛjuvaktrākṣināsaṃ
                        prasannacittavākceṣṭaṃ kleśasahaṃ ca bhiṣak śiṣyam upanayet ato
                        viparītaguṇaṃ nopanayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.4</label>
                        <caesura/> upanayanīyaṃ tu brāhmaṇaṃ praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu
                        praśastāyāṃ diśi śucau same deśe caturhastaṃ caturasraṃ sthaṇḍilam upalipya
                        gomayena darbhaiḥ saṃstīrya puṣpair lājabhaktai ratnaiś ca devatāḥ pūjayitvā
                        viprān bhiṣajaś ca tatrollikhyābhyukṣya ca dakṣiṇato brahmāṇaṃ
                        sthāpayitvā'gnim upasamādhāya khadirapalāśadevadārubilvānāṃ samidbhiś
                        caturṇāṃ vā kṣīravṛkṣāṇāṃ (? nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthamadhūkānāṃ )
                        dadhimadhughṛtāktābhir dārvīhaumikena vidhinā sruveṇājyāhutīr juhuyāt
                        sapraṇavābhir mahāvyahṛtibhiḥ tataḥ pratidaivatamṛṣīṃś ca svāhākāraṃ kuryāt
                        śiṣyam api kārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.5</label>
                        <caesura/> brāhmaṇas trayāṇāṃ varṇānām upanayanaṃ kartum arhati rājanyo
                        dvayasya vaiśyo vaiśyasyaiveti śūdram api kulaguṇasaṃpannaṃ mantravarjam
                        anupanītam adhyāpayed ity eke || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.6</label>
                        <caesura/> tato 'gniṃ triḥ pariṇīyāgnisākṣikaṃ śiṣyaṃ brūyāt
                        kāmakrodhalobhamohamānāhaṇkārerṣyāpāruṣyapaiśunyānṛtālasyāyaśasyāni hitvā
                        nīcanakharomṇā śucinā kaṣāyavāsasā
                        satyavratabrahmacaryābhivādanatatpareṇāvaśyaṃ bhavitavyaṃ
                        madanumatasthānagamanaśayanāsanabhojanādhyayanapareṇa bhūtvā matpriyahiteṣu
                        vartitavyaṃ ato 'nyathā te vartamānasyādharmo bhavati aphalā ca vidyā na ca
                        prākāśyaṃ prāpnoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.7</label>
                        <caesura/> ahaṃ vā tvayi samyagvartamāne yady anyathādarśī syām enobhāg
                        bhaveyam aphalavidyaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.8</label>
                        <caesura/> dvijagurudaridramitrapravrajitopanatasādhvanāthābhyupagatānāṃ
                        cātmabāndhavānām iva svabhaiṣajaiḥ pratikartavyam evaṃ sādhu bhavati
                        vyādhaśākunikapatitapāpakāriṇāṃ ca na pratikartavyaṃ evaṃ vidyā prakāśate
                            mitra<pc> </pc>yaśo<pc> </pc>dharmārtha<pc> </pc>kāmāṃś ca prāpnoti || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.9</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavataś cātra | kṛṣṇe 'ṣṭamī tannidhane 'hanī dve <caesura/>
                        śukle tathāpy evam ahar dvisandhyam | <caesura/> akālavidyutstanayitnughoṣe
                        <caesura/> svatantrarāṣṭrakṣitipavyathāsu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.2.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.2.10</label>
                        <caesura/> śmaśānayānādyatanāhaveṣu <caesura/> mahotsavautpātikadarśaneṣu |
                        <caesura/> nādhyeyam anyeṣu ca yeṣu vaprā <caesura/> nādhīyate nāśucinā ca
                        nityam || </l>

                    <p xml:id="SS1.2.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne śiṣyopanayanīyo nāma
                        dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                </div>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.3">

                        <caesura/> prāgabhihitaṃ saviṃśam adhyāyaśataṃ pañcasu sthāneṣu | tatra
                        sūtrasthānamadhyāyāḥ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśat ṣoḍśa nidānāni daśa śārīrāṇi
                        catvāriṃśaccikitsitāni aṣṭau kalpāḥ taduttaraṃ ṣaṭsāṣṭiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.4">

                        prabhāṣaṇāgraharaṇāvṛtucaryātha yāntrikaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.5">

                        agnikarmajalaukākhyāvadhyāyau raktavarṇanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.6">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.7">

                        kṛtyākṛtyavidhirvyādhisamuddeśīya eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.8">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.9">

                        vāraṇo yuktasenīya āturakramabhūnikau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.10">

                        dravyādīnāṃ ca vijñānaṃ viśeṣo dravyago 'paraḥ || </l>

                        pariniṣṭhitaḥ | <caesura/> sa muhyaty āturaṃ prāpya prāpya bhīrur ivāhavam
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.49">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.49</label>
                        <caesura/> yas tu karmasu niṣṇāto dhārṣṭyāc chāstrabahiṣkṛtaḥ | <caesura/>
                        sa satsu pūjāṃ nāpnoti vadhaṃ cārhati rājataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.50">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.50</label>
                        <caesura/> ubhāv etāv anipuṇāv asamarthau svakarmaṇi | <caesura/>
                        ardhavedadharāv etāv ekapakṣāv iva dvijau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.51">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.51</label>
                        <caesura/> oṣadhyo 'mṛtakalpās tu śastrāśaniviṣopamāḥ | <caesura/> bhavanty
                        ajñair upahṛtās tasmād etān vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.52">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.52</label>
                        <caesura/> snehādiṣv anabhijñā ye chedyādiṣu ca karmasu | <caesura/> te
                        nihanti janaṃ lobhāt kuvaidyā nṛpadoṣataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.53">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.53</label>
                        <caesura/> yas tūbhayajño matimān sa samartho 'rthasādhane | <caesura/>
                        āhave karma nirvoḍhuṃ dvicakraḥ syandano yathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.54">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.54</label>
                        <caesura/> atha vatsa tad etad adhyeyaṃ tathā tathopadhāraya mayā
                        procyamānaṃ atha śucaye kṛtottarāsaṅgāyāvyākulayopasthitāyādhyayanakāle
                        śiṣyāya yathāśakti gurur upadiśet padaṃ pādaṃ ślokaṃ vā te ca
                        padapādaślokābhūyaḥ krameṇānusaṃdheyāḥ evam ekaikaśo ghaṭayed ātmanā
                        cānupaṭhet adrutam avilambitam aviśaṇkitam ananunāsikaṃ vyaktākṣram
                        apīḍitavarṇam akṣibhruvauṣṭhahastair anabhinītaṃ susaṃskṛtaṃ nātyuccair
                        nātinīcaiś ca svaraiḥ paṭhet | na cāntareṇa kaścid vrajet tayor adhīyānayoḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.55">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.55</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavataś cātra | <caesura/> śucir guruparo dakṣas
                        tandrānidrāvivarjitaḥ | <caesura/> paṭhann etena vidhinā śiṣyaḥ śāstrāntam
                        āpnuyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.3.56">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.3.56</label>
                        <caesura/> vāksauṣṭhave 'rthavijñāne prāgalbhye karmanaipuṇe | <caesura/>
                        tadabhyāse ca siddhau ca yatetādhyayanāntagaḥ || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāhaṃ sūtrasthāne 'dhyayanasaṃpradānīyo nāma
                        tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="4" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaḥ prabhāṣaṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yāthovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.3</label>
                        <caesura/> adhigatam apy adhyayanam aprabhāṣitam arthataḥ kharasya
                        candanabhāra iva kevalaṃ pariśramakaraṃ bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.4</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> yathā kharaś candanabhāravāhī bhārasya
                        vettā na tu candanasya | <caesura/> evaṃ hi śāstrāṇi baḥūny adhītya cārtheṣu
                        mūḍhāḥ kharavad vahanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.5</label>
                        <caesura/> tasmāt saviṃśam adhyāyaśatam anupadapādaślokam anuvarṇayitavyam
                        anuśrotavyaṃ ca kasmāt sūkṣmā hi
                        dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākadoṣadhātumalāśayamarmasirāsnāyusandhyasthigarbhasaṃbhavadravyasamūhavibhāgās
                        tathā pranaṣṭaśalyoddharaṇavraṇaviniścayabhagnavikalpāḥ sādhyayāpy
                        apratyākhyeyatā ca vikārāṇām evam ādayaś cānye sahasraśo viśeṣā ye
                        vicintyamānā vimalavipulabuddher api buddhim ākulīkuryuḥ kiṃ punar
                        alpabuddheḥ tasmād avaśyam anupadapādaślokam anuvarṇayitavyam anuśrotavyaṃ
                        ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.6</label>
                        <caesura/> anyaśāstropapannānāṃ cārthānām ihopanītānām arthavaśāt teṣāṃ tad
                        vidyebhya eva vyākhyānam anuśrotavyaṃ kasmāt na hy ekasmin śāstre śakyaḥ
                        sarvaśāstrāṇām avarodhaḥ kartum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.7</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra | <caesura/> ekaṃ śāstram adhīyāno na vidyāc
                        chāstraniścayam | <caesura/> tasmād bahuśrutaḥ śāstraṃ vijānīyāc cikitsakaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.8</label>
                        <caesura/> śāstraṃ gurumukhodgīrṇam ādāyopāsya cāsakṛt | <caesura/> yaḥ
                        karma kurute vaiyaḥ sa vaidyo 'nye tu taskarāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.4.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.4.9</label>
                        <caesura/> aupadhenavam aurabhraṃ sauśrutaṃ pauṣkalāvatam | <caesura/>
                        śeṣāṇāṃ śalyatantrāṇāṃ mūlāny etāni nirdiśet || </l>

                    <p ana="1.4.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne prabhāṣanīyo nāma
                        caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="6" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>śaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāta ṛtucaryam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.3</label>
                        <caesura/> kālo hi nāma bhagavān svayambhur anādimadhyanidhano 'tra
                        rasavyāpatsampattī jīvitamaraṇe ca manuṣyāṇām āyatte | sa sūkṣmām api kalāṃ
                        na līyata iti kālaḥ saṃkalayati kālayati vā bhūtānīti kālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.4</label>
                        <caesura/> tasya saṃvatsarātmano bhagavān ādityo gativiśeṣeṇa
                        nimeṣakāṣṭhākalāmuhūrtāhorātrapakṣamāsartvayanasaṃvatsarayugapravibhāgaṃ
                        karoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.5</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra laghvakṣaroccāraṇamātro 'kṣinimeṣaḥ pañcadaśā'kṣinimeṣāḥ
                        kāṣṭhā triṃśatkāṣṭhāḥ kalā viṃśatikalo muhūrtaḥ kalādaśabhāgaś ca
                        triṃśanmuhūrtam ahorātraṃ pañcadaśāhorātrāṇi pakṣaḥ sa ca dvividhaḥ śuklaḥ
                        kṛṣṇaś ca tau māsaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.6</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra māghādayo dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ dvimāsikam ṛtuṃ kṛtva
                        ṣaḍṛtavo bhavanti te śiśiravasantagrīṣmavarṣāśaraddhemantāḥ teṣaṃ
                        tapastapsyau śiśiraḥ madhumādhavau vasantaḥ śuciśukrau grīṣmaḥ
                        nabhonabhasyau varśāḥ iṣorjau śarat sahaḥsahasyau hemanta iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.7</label>
                        <caesura/> ta ete śītoṣṇavarṣalakṣaṇāś candrād ity ayoḥ kālavibhāgakaratvād
                        ayane dve bhavato dakṣiṇam uttaraṃ ca | tayor dakṣiṇaṃ varṣāśaraddhemantāḥ
                        teṣu bhagavān āpyāyate somaḥ amlalavaṇamadhurāś ca rasā balavanto bhavanti
                        uttarottaraṃ ca sarvaprāṇināṃ balam abhivardhate | uttaraṃ ca
                        śiśiravasantagrīṣmāḥ teṣu bhagavān āpyāyate 'rkaḥ tiktakaṣāyakaṭukāś ca rasā
                        balavanto bhavanti uttarottaraṃ ca sarvaprāṇināṃ balam apahīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.8</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> śītāṃśuḥ kledayaty urvīṃ vivasvān
                        śoṣayaty api | <caesura/> tāv ubhāv api saṃśritya vāyuḥ pālayati prajāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.9</label>
                        <caesura/> atha khalv ayane dve yugapat saṃvatsaro bhavati te tu pañca yugam
                        iti saṃjñāṃ labhante sa eṣa nimeṣādir yugaparyantaḥ kālaś cakravat
                        parivartamānaḥ kālacakram ucyata ity eke || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.10</label>
                        <caesura/> iha tu varṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmaprāvṛṣaḥ ṣaḍṛtavo bhavanti
                        doṣopacayaprakopopaśamanimittaṃ te tu bhādrapadādyena dvimāsikena vyākhyātāḥ
                        tad yathā bhādrapadāśvayujau varṣāḥ kārtikamārgaśīrṣau śarat pauṣamāghau
                        hemantaḥ phālgunacaitrau vasantaḥ vaiśākhajyeṣṭhau grīṣmaḥ āṣāḍhaśrāvaṇau
                        prāvṛḍ iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.6.11</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra varṣāsv oṣadhayas taruṇyo 'lpavīryā āpaś cāprasannāḥ
                        kṣitimalaprāyāḥ tā upayujyamānā nabhasi meghāvatate jalapraklinnāyāṃ bhūmau
                        klinnadehānāṃ prāṇināṃ śīta<pc> </pc>vāta<pc> </pc>viṣṭambhitāgnīnāṃ
                        vidahyante vidāhāt pittasaṃcayam āpādayanti sa saṃcayaḥ śaradi
                        praviralameghe viyaty upaśuṣyati paṅke 'rka<pc> </pc>kiraṇa<pc
                        > </pc>pravilāyitaḥ paittikān vyādhīn janayati | tā evauṣadhayaḥ
                        kālapariṇāmāt pariṇatavīryā balavatyo hemante bhavanty āpaś ca prasannāḥ
                        snigdhā atyarthaṃ gurvyaś ca tā upayujyamānā mandakiraṇatvād bhānoḥ
                            satuṣārapa<pc> </pc>vanopa<pc> </pc>stambhita<pc> </pc>dehānāṃ dehinām
                        avidagdhāḥ snehāc chaityād gauravād upalepāc ca śleṣmasaṃcayam āpādayanti sa
                        saṃcayo vasante 'rka<pc> </pc>raśmi<pc> </pc>pravilāyita īṣatstabdhadehānāṃ
                        dehināṃ ślaiṣmikān vyādhīn janayati | tā evauṣadhayo nidāghe niḥsārā rūkṣā
                        atimātraṃ laghvyo bhavanty āpaś ca tā upayujyamānāḥ
                        sūryapratāpopaśoṣitadehānāṃ dehināṃ raukṣyāl laghutvād vaiśadyāc ca vāyoḥ
                        saṃcayam āpādayanti sa saṃcayaḥ prāvṛṣi cātyarthaṃ jalopaklinnāyāṃ bhūmau
                        klinnadehānāṃ prāṇināṃ śītavātavarṣerito vātikān vyādhīn janayati | evam eṣa
                        doṣāṇāṃ saṃcayaprakopahetur uktaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.6.15">

                        upalakṣayet evam ahorātram api varṣam iva śītoṣṇavarṣalakṣaṇaṃ
                        doṣopacayaprakopopaśamair jānīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.17</label>
                        <caesura/> yantrakarmāṇi tu
                        nirghātanapūraṇabandhanavyūhanavartanacālanavivartanavivaraṇapīḍanamārgaviśodhanavikarṣaṇāharaṇāñchanonnamanavinamanabhañjanonmathanācūṣaṇaiṣaṇadāraṇarjūkaraṇaprakṣālanapradhamanapramārjanāni
                        caturviṃśatiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.18</label>
                        <caesura/> svabuddhyā cāpi vibhajedyantrakarmāṇi buddhimān | <caesura/>
                        asaṃkhyeyavikalpatvāc chalyānām iti niścayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.19</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra atisthūlaṃ asāraṃ atidīrghaṃ atihrasvaṃ agrāhi viṣamagrāhi
                        vakraṃ śithilaṃ atyunnataṃ mṛdukīlaṃ mṛdumukhaṃ mṛdupāśam iti dvādaśa
                        yantradoṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.20</label>
                        <caesura/> etair doṣair vinirmuktaṃ yantramaṣṭādaśāṅgulam | <caesura/>
                        praśastaṃ bhiṣajā jñeyaṃ taddhi karmasu yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.21</label>
                        <caesura/> dṛśyaṃ siṃhamukhādyais tu gūḍhaṃ kaṅkamukhādibhiḥ | <caesura/>
                        nirharet tu śanaiḥ śalyaṃ śa(ā.śā)strayuktivyapekṣayā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.7.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.7.22</label>
                        <caesura/> ni(ā.vi)vartate sādhvavagāhate ca śalyaṃ nigṛhyoddharate ca
                        yasmāt || <caesura/> yantreṣv ataḥ kaṅkamukhaṃ pradhānaṃ sthāneṣu sarveṣv
                        adhi(ā.vi)kāri caiva || </l>
                    <l ana="SS.1.7.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne yantravidhirnāma
                        saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||</l>
                </div>

                <div n="8" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>aṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaḥ śastrāvacāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.3</label>
                        <caesura/> viṃśatiḥ śastrāṇi; tad yathā— maṇḍalāgrakarapatra<pc
                            > </pc>vṛddhipatra<pc> </pc>nakhaśastra<pc
                            > </pc>mudrikotpalapatrakārdhadhāra<pc> </pc>sūcī<pc
                            > </pc>kuśapatrāṭīmukha<pc> </pc>śarārimukhāntarmukha<pc
                            > </pc>trikūrcaka<pc> </pc>kuṭhārikā<pc> </pc>vrīhimukhārā<pc
                            > </pc>vetasapatraka<pc> </pc>baḍiśa<pc> </pc>dantaśaṅkveṣaṇya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.4</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra maṇḍalāgrakarapatre syātāṃ chedane lekhane ca,
                            vṛddhipatra<pc> </pc>nakhaśastra<pc> </pc>mudrikotpalapatrakārdhadhārāṇi
                        chedane bhedane ca, sūcīkuśapatrāṭī(ṭā)mukhaśarārimukhāntarmukhatrikūrcakāni
                        visrāvaṇe, kuṭhārikā<pc> </pc>vrīhimukhārā<pc> </pc>vetasapatrakāṇi vyadhane
                        sūcī ca, baḍiśaṃ dantaśaṅkuś cāharaṇe, eṣaṇy eṣaṇe ānulomye ca sūcyaḥ
                        sīvane; ity aṣṭavidhe karmaṇy upayogaḥ śastrāṇāṃ vyākkhyātaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.5</label>
                        <caesura/> teṣām atha yathāyogaṃ grahaṇasamāsopāyaḥ karmasu vakṣyate— tatra
                        vṛddhipatraṃ vṛntaphalasādhāraṇe bhāge gṛhṇīyāt, bhedanāny evaṃ sarvāṇi,
                        vṛddhipatraṃ maṇḍalāgraṃ ca kiṃcid uttānena pāṇinā lekhane bahuśo 'vacāryaṃ,
                        vṛntāgre visrāvaṇāni, viśeṣeṇa tu bālavṛddhasukumārabhīrunārīṇāṃ rājñāṃ
                        rājamā(pu)trāṇāṃ ca trikūrcakena visrāvayet, talapracchādita<pc> </pc>vṛntam
                        aṅguṣṭhapradeśinībhyāṃ vrīhimukhaṃ, kuṭhārikāṃ vāmahastanyastām
                            itarahastamadhyamāṅgulyā'ṅguṣṭhaviṣṭabdhay<pc> </pc>'bhihanyāt,
                        ārākarapatraiṣaṇyo mūle, śeṣāṇi tu yathāyogaṃ gṛhṇīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.6</label>
                        <caesura/> teṣāṃ nāmabhir evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.7-8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.7-8</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra nakhaśastraiṣaṇyāv aṣṭāṅgule, sūcyo vakṣyante,
                        (pradeśinyagraparvapradeśapramāṇā mudrikā, daśāṅgulā śarārimukhī sā ca (yā
                        sā) kartarīti kathyate |), śeṣāṇi tu ṣaḍaṅgulāni || tāni sugrahāṇi sulohāni
                        sudhārāṇi surūpāṇi susamāhitamukhāgrāṇi akarālāni ceti śastrasaṃpat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.9</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra vakraṃ, kuṇṭhaṃ, khaṇḍaṃ, kharadhāram, atisthūlam,
                        atyalpam, atidīrgham, atihrasvam, ity aṣṭau śastradoṣāḥ | ato viparītaguṇam
                        ādadīta, anyatra karapatrāt; tad dhi kharadhāram asthicchedanārtham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.10</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra dhārā bhedanānāṃ māsūrī, lekhanānām ardhamāsūrī,
                        vyadhanānāṃ visrāvaṇānāṃ ca kaiśikī, chedanānām ardhakaiśikīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.11</label>
                        <caesura/> baḍiśaṃ dantaśaṅkuś cānatāgre |
                        tīkṣṇakaṇṭakaprathamayavapatramukhyeṣaṇī (gaṇḍūpadākāramukhī ca) || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.12</label>
                        <caesura/> teṣāṃ pāyanā trividhā kśārodakataileṣu | tatra kṣārapāyitaṃ
                        śaraśalyāsthicchedaneṣu udakapāyitaṃ māṃsacchedanabhedanapāṭaneṣu
                        tailapāyitaṃ sirāvyadhanasnāyucchedaneṣu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.13</label>
                        <caesura/> teṣāṃ niśānārthaṃ ślakṣṇaśilā māṣavarṇā dhārāsaṃsthāpanārthaṃ
                        śālmalīphalakam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.14</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra— <caesura/> yadā suniśitaṃ śastraṃ romacchedi
                        susaṃsthitam | <caesura/> sugṛhītaṃ pramāṇena tadā karmasu yojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.15</label>
                        <caesura/> anuśastrāṇi tu tvaksāra<pc> </pc>sphaṭika<pc> </pc>kāca<pc
                            > </pc>kuruvinda<pc> </pc>jalaukogni<pc
                        > </pc>kṣāranakhagojīśephālikāśākapatrakarīrabālāṅgulaya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.16</label>
                        <caesura/> śiśūnāṃ śastrabhīrūṇāṃ śastrābhāve ca yojayet | <caesura/>
                        tvaksārādicaturvargaṃ chedye ca buddhimān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.17</label>
                        <caesura/> āhārya<pc> </pc>cchedya<pc> </pc>bhedyeṣu nakhaṃ śakyeṣu yojayet
                        | <caesura/> vidhiḥ pravakṣyate paścāt kṣāravahnijalaukasām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.18</label>
                        <caesura/> ye syur mukhagatā rogā netravartmagatāś ca ye | <caesura/>
                            gojī<pc> </pc>śephālikā<pc> </pc>śākapatrair visrāvayet tu tān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.19</label>
                        <caesura/> eṣyeṣv eṣaṇyalābhe tu bālāṅgulyaṅkurā hitāḥ || <caesura/>
                        śastrāṇy etāni matimān śuddhaśaikyāyasāni tu || <caesura/> kārayet
                        karaṇaprāptaṃ karmāraṃ karmakovidam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.8.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.8.20</label>
                        <caesura/> prayogajñasya vaidyasya siddhir bhavati nity aśaḥ | <caesura/>
                        tasmāt paricayaṃ kuryāc chastrāṇāṃ grahaṇe sadā || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne śastrāvacāraṇīyo nāmāṣṭamo
                        'dhyāyaḥ ||</p>

                <div n="9" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>navamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāto yogyāsūtrīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.3</label>
                        <caesura/> adhigatasarvaśāstrārtham api śiṣyaṃ yogyāṃ kārayet | snehādiṣu
                        chedyādīṣu ca karmapatham upadiśet | subahuśruto 'pyakṛtayogyaḥ
                        karmasvayogyo bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.4</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra
                        puṣpaphalālābūkālindakatrapusai(ā.so)rvārukarkārukaprabhṛtiṣu chedyaviśeṣān
                        darśayet utkartanaparikartanāni copadiśet
                        dṛtibastiprasevakaprabhṛtiṣūdakapaṅkapūrṇeṣu bhedyayogyāṃ saromṇi
                        carmaṇyātate lekhyasya mṛtapaśusirāsūtpalanāleṣu ca vedhyasya
                        ghuṇopahatakāṣṭhaveṇunalanālīśuṣkālābūmukheṣveṣyasya
                        panasabimbībilvaphalamajjamṛtapaśudanteṣvāhāryasya madhūcchiṣṭopalipte
                        śālmalīphalake visrāvyasya sūkṣmaghanavastrāntayor mṛducarmāntayoś ca
                        sīvyasya pustamayapuruśāṅgapratyaṅgaviśeṣeṣu bandhanayogyāṃ
                        mṛducarmamāṃsapeśīṣūtpalanāleṣu ca karṇasandhibandhayogyāṃ mṛduṣu
                        māṃsakhaṇḍeṣv agnikṣārayogyāṃ udakapūṇaghaṭapārśvasrotasyalābūmukhādiṣu ca
                        netrapraṇidhānabastivraṇabastipīḍanayogyām iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.5ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.5ab</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavataś cātra | <caesura/> evam ādiṣu medhāvī yogyārheṣu
                        yathāvidhi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.5cd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.5cd</label>
                        <caesura/> dravyeṣu yogyāṃ kurvāṇo na pramuhyati karmasu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.6ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.6ab</label>
                        <caesura/> tasmāt kauśalam anvicchan śastrakṣārāgnikarmasu |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.9.6cd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.9.6cd</label>
                        <caesura/> yasya yatreha sādharmyaṃ tatra yogyāṃ samācaret || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne yogyāsūtrīyo nāma navamo
                        'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                </div>



                <div n="10" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāto viśikhānupraveśanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.3</label>
                        <caesura/> adhigatatantreṇopāsitatantrārthena dṛṣṭakarmaṇā kṛtayogyena
                        śāstraṃ nigadatā rājānujñātena nīcanakharomṇā ṣucinā śuklavastraparihitena
                        chatravatā daṇḍahastena sopānatkenānuddhataveśena sumanasā
                        kalyāṇābhivyāhāreṇākuhakena bandhubhūtena bhūtānāṃ susahāyavatā vaidyena
                        niśikhā'nupraveṣṭavyā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.4.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.4.1</label>
                        <caesura/> tato dūtanimittaśakunamaṅgalānulomyenātura<pc> </pc>gṛham
                        abhigamya, upaviśya, āturam abhipaśyet spṛśet pṛcchec ca; tribhir etair
                        vijñānopāyai rogāḥ prāyaśo veditavyā </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.4.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.4.2</label>
                        <caesura/> ity eke tat tu na samyak ṣaḍvidho hi rogāṇāṃ vijñānopāyaḥ; tad
                        yathā --- pañcabhiḥ śrotrādibhiḥ praśnena ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.5</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra śrotrendriyavijñeyā viśeṣā rogeṣu vraṇāsrāvanijñānīyādiṣu
                        vakṣyante tatra saphenaṃ raktam īrayann anilaḥ saśabdo nirgacchati ity evam
                        ādayaḥ sparśanendriyavijñeyāḥ śītoṣṇaślakṣṇakarkaśamṛdukaṭhinatvād ayaḥ
                        sparśaviśeṣā jvaraśophādeṣu cakṣurindriyavijñeyāḥ
                        śarīropacayāpacayāyurlakṣaṇabalavarṇavikārādayaḥ rasanendriyavijñeyāḥ
                        pramehādiṣu rasaviśeṣāḥ ghrāṇendriyavijñeyā ariṣṭaliṅgādiṣu vraṇānām
                        avraṇānāṃ ca gandhaviśeṣāḥ praśnena ca vijānīyād deśaṃ kālaṃ jātiṃ sātmyam
                        ātaṅkasamutpattiṃ vedanāsamucchrāyaṃ balam antaragniṃ vātamūtrapurīṣāṇāṃ
                        pravṛttyapravṛttī kālaprakarṣādīṃś ca viśeṣān | ātmasadṛśeṣu
                        vijñānābhyupāyeṣu tatsthānīyair jānīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.6</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> mithyādṛṣṭā vikārā hi durākhyātās
                        tathaiva ca | <caesura/> tathā duṣparimṛṣṭāś ca mohayeyuś cikitsakam || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.6ef</label>
                        <caesura/> yāpayet asādhyān nopakramet parisaṃvatsarotthitāṃś ca vikārān
                        prāyaśo varjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.8</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra sādhyā api vyādhayaḥ prāyeṇaiṣāṃ duścikitsyatamā bhavanti |
                        tad yathā śrotriyanṛpatistrībālavṛddhabhīru<pc> </pc>rājasevaka<pc
                            > </pc>kitavadrubala<pc> </pc>vaidyavidagdha<pc
                            > </pc>vyādhigopaka<pc> </pc>daridra<pc> </pc>kṛpaṇa<pc
                        > </pc>krodhanānām anātmavatām anāthānāṃ ca evaṃ nirūpya cikitsāṃ kurvan
                        dharmārthakāmayaśāṃsi prāpnoti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.9</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> strībhiḥ sahāsyāṃ saṃvāsaṃ parihāsaṃ
                        ca varjayet | <caesura/> dattaṃ ca tābhyo nādeyam annād anyad bhiṣagvaraiḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.10.trailer">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.10.trailer</label>
                        <caesura/> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne viśikhānupraveśanīyo nāma
                        daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>

                <div n="11" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaḥ kṣārapākavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.3</label>
                        <caesura/> śastrānuśastrebhyaḥ kṣāraḥ pradhānatamaḥ
                        chedyabhedyalekhyakaraṇāt tridoṣaghnatvād viśeṣakriyāvacāraṇāc ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.4</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra kṣaraṇāt kṣaṇanād vā kṣāraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.5</label>
                        <caesura/> nānauṣadhisamavāyāt tridoṣaghnaḥ śuklatvāt saumyaḥ tasya
                        saumyasyāpi sato dahanapacanadāraṇādiśaktiraviruddhā sa khalv
                        āgneyauṣadhiguṇabhūyiṣṭhatvāt kaṭuka uṣṇastīkṣṇaḥ pa(ā.pā)cano vilayanaḥ
                        śodhano ropaṇaḥ śoṣaṇaḥ stambhano lekhanaḥ kṛmyāmakaphakuṣṭhaviṣamedasām
                        upahantā puṃstvasya cātisevitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.6</label>
                        <caesura/> sa dvividhaḥ pratisāraṇīyaḥ pānīyaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.7</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra pratisāraṇīyaḥ kuṣṭha<pc> </pc>kiṭibha<pc
                            > </pc>dadru<pc> </pc>maṇḍala<pc> </pc>kilāsa<pc
                            > </pc>bhagandarārbudārśo<pc> </pc>duṣṭa<pc> </pc>vraṇa<pc
                            > </pc>nāḍī<pc> </pc>carma<pc> </pc>kīla<pc
                            > </pc>tilakālakanyaccha<pc> </pc>vyaṅga<pc> </pc>maśaka<pc
                            > </pc>bāhya<pc> </pc>vidradhi<pc> </pc>kṛmi<pc> </pc>viṣādiṣūpadiśyate
                        saptasu ca mukharogeṣūpajihvādhijihvopakuśadantavaidarbheṣu tisṛṣu ca
                        rohiṇīṣu eteṣv evānuśastra<pc> </pc>praṇidhānam uktam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.8</label>
                        <caesura/> pānīyas tu
                        garagulmodarāgnisaṅgājīrṇārocakānāhaśarkarāśmaryābhyantaravidradhikṛmiviṣārśaḥsūpayujyate

                        raktapitta(ā.tti)jvaritapittaprakṛtibālavṛddhadurbalabhramamadamūrcchātimiraparītebhyo
                        'nyebhyaś caivaṃvidhebhyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.10">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.11</label>
                        <caesura/> athetaras trividho mṛdurmadhyastīkṣṇaś ca | taṃ cikīrṣuḥ śaradi
                        girisānujaṃ śucir upoṣya praśaste 'hani praśastadeśajātam anupahataṃ
                        madhyamavayasaṃ mahāntamasitamuṣkakamadhivāsyāparedyuḥ pāṭayitvā svaṇḍaśaḥ
                        prakalpyāvapāṭya nirvāte deśe nicitiṃ kṛtvā sudhāśarkarāś ca prakṣipya
                        nilanālair ādīpayet | athopaśānte 'gnau tadbhasma
                        pṛthaggṛhṇīyādbhasmaśarkarāś ca | athānenaiva vidhānena
                        kuṭajapalāśāśvakarṇapāribhadrakabibhītakāragvadhatilvakārkasnuhyapāmārgapāṭalānaktamālavṛṣakadalīcitrakapūtīkendravṛkṣāsphotāśvamārakasaptacchadāgnimanthaguñjāś
                        catasraś ca kośātakīḥ samūlaphalapatraśākhā dahet | tataḥ kṣāradroṇam
                        udakadroṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhir āloḍya mūtrair vā yathoktair ekaviṃśatikṛtvaḥ
                        parisrāvya mahati kaṭāhe śanair darvyāvaghaṭṭayan vipacet | sa yadā bhavaty
                        accho raktas tīkṣṇaḥ picchilaś ca tamādāya mahati vastre parisrāvyetaraṃ
                        vibhajya punar agnāv adhiśrayet | tata eva cakṣārodakāt kuḍavamadhyardhaṃ
                        vā'panayet | tataḥ kaṭaśarkarābhasmaśarkarākṣīrapākaśaṅkhanābhīragnivarṇāḥ
                        kṛtvā+āyase pātre tasminn eva kṣārodake niṣicya piṣṭvā </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.11.11b">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.11.11b</label>
                        <caesura/> tenaiva dvidroṇe 'ṣṭapalasaṃmitaṃ śaṅkhānābhyādīnāṃ pramāṇaṃ
                        prativāpya satatam aprmattaś cainam avaghaṭṭayan vipacet | sa yathā
                        nātisāndro nātidravaś ca bhavati tathā prayateta | athainam āgatapākam
                        avatāryānuguptam āyase kumbhe saṃvṛtamukhe nidadhyād eṣa madhyamaḥ || </l>

                         madhūcchiṣṭaṃ samadhukaṃ rodhraṃ sarjarasaṃ tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.28</label>
                        <caesura/> mañjiṣṭhāṃ cadanaṃ mūrvāṃ piṣṭvā sarpir vipācayet | <caesura/>
                        sarveṣāmagnidagdhānām etad ropaṇam uttamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.29ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.29ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehadagdhe kriyāṃ rūkṣāṃ viśeṣeṇāvacārayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.29cd">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.12.29cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi dhūmopahatalakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.30</label>
                        <caesura/> śvasiti kṣauti cātyarthamatyādhamati kāsate | <caesura/> cakṣuṣoḥ
                        paridāhaś ca rāgaś caivopajāyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.31</label>
                        <caesura/> sadhūmakaṃ niśvasiti ghreyamanyanna vetti ca | <caesura/>
                        tathaiva ca rasān sarvān śrutiś cāsyopahanyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.32abc">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.32abc</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṣṇādāhajvarayutaḥ sīdatyatha ca mūrcchati |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmopahata ity evaṃ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.32d">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.12.32d</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śṛṇu tasya cikitsitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.33">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.33</label>
                        <caesura/> sarpirikṣurasaṃ drākṣāṃ payo vā śarkarāmbu vā | <caesura/>
                        madhurāmlau rasau vā'pi vamanāya pradāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.34">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.34</label>
                        <caesura/> vamataḥ koṣṭhaśuddhiḥ syāddhūmagandhaś ca naśyati | <caesura/>
                        vidhinā'nena śāmyanti sadanakṣavathujvarāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.35">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dāha<pc> </pc>mūrcchā<pc> </pc>tṛḍādhmāna<pc> </pc>śvāsakāsāś ca dāruṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         madhurair lavaṇāmlaiś ca kaṭukaiḥ kavalagrahaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.36ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.36ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samyag gṛhṇātīndriyārthān manaś cāsya prasīdati |</l>
                      
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.36cd">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.12.36cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirecanaṃ cāsmai dadyād yogena śāstravit || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭir viśudhyate cāsya śirogrīvaṃ ca dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         avidāhi laghu snigdhamāhāraṃ cāsya kalpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.38ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.12.38ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇavātātapair dagdhe śītaḥ kāryo vidhiḥ sadā |</l>
                    
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.38cd">

                        <caesura/>
                         śītavarṣānilair dagdhe snigdhamuṣṇaṃ ca śasyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.39ab">

                         tathā'titejasā dagdhe siddhir nāsti kathaṃcana |</l>
                    
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.12.39cdef">

                        <caesura/>
                         indravajrāgnidaghe 'pi jīvati pratikārayet || </l>

                        dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>

                <div n="13" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <note>The vulgate text here in adhyāya 13 is transcribed from the 1938 edition,
                        not the 1931 edition.</note>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.1">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāto jalaukāvacāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.2">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.3">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.3</label>
                        <caesura/> nṛpāḍhya<pc> </pc>bāla<pc> </pc>sthavira<pc> </pc>bhīru<pc
                            > </pc>durbala<pc> </pc>nārī<pc> </pc>sukumārāṇām anugrahārthaṃ
                        paramasukumāro 'yaṃ śoṇitāvasecanopāyo 'bhihito jalaukasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.4">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.4</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra vātapittakaphaduṣṭaśoṇitaṃ yathāsaṃkhyaṃ
                        śṛṅgajalaukālābubhir avasecayet sarvāṇi sarvair vā (viśeṣas tu visrāvyaṃ
                        śṛṅgajalaukālābubhir gṛhṇīyāt) || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.5">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.5</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ | <caesura/> uṣṇaṃ samadhuraṃ snigdhaṃ
                        gavāṃ śṛṅgaṃ prakīrtitam | <caesura/> tasmād vātopasṛṣṭe tu hitaṃ tad
                        avasecane || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.6">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.6</label>
                        <caesura/> śītādhivāsā madhurā jalaukā vārisaṃbhavā | <caesura/> tasmāt
                        pittopasṛṣṭe tu hitā sā tv avasecane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.7">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.7</label>
                        <caesura/> alābu kaṭukaṃ rūkṣaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ ca parikīrtitam | <caesura/> tasmāc
                        chleṣmopasṛṣṭe tu hitaṃ tad avasecane || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.8">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.8</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra pracchite tanu<pc> </pc>basti<pc> </pc>paṭalāvanaddhena
                        śṛṅgeṇa śoṇitam avasecayed ācūṣaṇāt sāntardīpayā 'lābvā | (jalāyukā
                        vakṣyante) || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.9">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.9</label>
                        <caesura/> jalam āsām āyur iti jalāyukāḥ jalam āsām oka iti jalaukasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.10">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.10</label>
                        <caesura/> tā dvādaśa tāsāṃ saviṣāḥ ṣaṭ tāvatya eva nirviṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.11">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.11</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra saviṣāḥ kṛṣṇā karburā alagardā indrāyudhā sāmudrikā
                        gocandanā ceti | tāsu añjanacūrṇavarṇā pṛthuśirāḥ kṛṣṇā varmimatsyavad āyatā
                        chinnonnatakukṣiḥ karburā romaśā mahāpārśvā kṛṣṇamukhī alagardā
                        indrāyudhavad ūrdhvarājibhiś citritā indrāyudhā īṣadasitapītikā
                        vicitrapuṣpākṛticitrā sāmudrikāḥ govṛṣaṇavad adhobhāge dvidhābhūtākṛtir
                        aṇumukhī gocandaneti | tābhir daṣṭe puruṣe daṃśe śvayathur atimātraṃ
                        kaṇḍūrmūrcchā jvaro dāhaś chardir madaḥ sadanam iti liṅgāni bhavanti | tatra
                        mahāgadaḥ pānālepananasya karmādiṣūpayojyaḥ | indrāyudhādaṣṭam asādhyam |
                        ity etāḥ saviṣāḥ sacikitsitā vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.12">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.12</label>
                        <caesura/> atha nirviṣāḥ kapilā piṅgalā śaṅkumukhī mūṣikā puṇḍarīkamukhī
                        sāvarikā ceti | tatra manaḥśilārañjitābhyām iva pārśvābhyāṃ pṛṣṭhe snigdhā
                        mudgavarṇā kapilā kiṃcidraktā vṛttakāyā piṅgalā ''śugā ca piṅgalā yakṛdvarṇā
                        śīghrapāyinī dīrghatīkṣṇamukhī śaṅkumukhīḥ mūṣikākṛtivarṇā 'niṣṭagandhā ca
                        mūṣikā mudgavarṇā puṇḍarīkatulyavaktrā puṇḍarīkamukhī snigdhā
                        padmapatravarṇā 'ṣṭādaśāṅgulapramāṇā sāvarikā sā ca paśvarthe ity etā aviṣā
                        vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.13">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.13</label>
                        <caesura/> tāsāṃ yavanapāṇḍyasahya<pc> </pc>pautanādīni kṣetrāṇi teṣu
                        mahāśarīrā balavatyaḥ śīghrapāyinyo mahāśanā nirviṣāś ca viśeṣeṇa bhavanti
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.14">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.14</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra saviṣa<pc> </pc>matsya<pc> </pc>kīṭa<pc
                            > </pc>dardura<pc> </pc>mūtra<pc> </pc>purīṣa<pc> </pc>kothajātāḥ
                        kaluṣeṣv ambhaḥsu ca saviṣāḥ padmotpala<pc> </pc>nalina<pc
                            > </pc>kumuda<pc> </pc>saugandhika<pc> </pc>kuvalaya<pc
                            > </pc>puṇḍarīka<pc> </pc>śaivala<pc> </pc>kotha<pc> </pc>jātā vimaleṣv
                        ambhaḥsu ca nirviṣāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.15">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.15</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> kṣetreṣu vicaranty etāḥ
                        salilāḍhyasugandhiṣu | <caesura/> na ca saṃkīrṇacāriṇyo na ca paṅkeśayāḥ
                        sukhāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.16">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.16</label>
                        <caesura/> tāsāṃ grahaṇam ārdracarmaṇā, anyair vā prayogair gṛhṇīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.17">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.17</label>
                        <caesura/> athaināṃ nave mahati ghaṭe sarastaḍāgodakapaṅkam āvāpya nidadhyāt
                        bhakṣyārthe cāsām upaharec chaivalaṃ vallūram audakāṃś ca kandāṃś cūrṇīkṛtya
                        śayyārthaṃ tṛṇam audakāni ca patrāṇi tryahāt tryahāc cābhyo 'nyaj jalaṃ
                        bhakṣyaṃ ca dadyāt saptarātrāt saptarātrāc ca ghaṭam anyaṃ saṃkrāmayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.18">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.18</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> sthūlamadhyāḥ parikliṣṭāḥ pṛthvyo
                        mandaviceṣṭitāḥ | <caesura/> agrāhiṇyo 'lpapāyinyaḥ saviṣāś ca na pūjitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.19">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.19</label>
                        <caesura/> atha jalauko 'vasekasādhyavyādhitam upaveśya saṃveśya vā virūkṣya
                        cāsya tam avakāśaṃ mṛdgomayacūrṇair yady arujaḥ syāt | gṛhītāś ca tāḥ
                            sarṣaparajanī<pc> </pc>kalkodaka<pc> </pc>pradigdha<pc> </pc>gātrīḥ
                        salilasarakamadhye muhūrtasthitā vigataklamā jñātvā tābhī rogaṃ grāhayet |
                        ślakṣṇaśuklārdrapicuprotāvacchannāṃ kṛtvā mukham apāvṛṇuyāt agṛhṇantyai
                        kṣīrabinduṃ śoṇitabinduṃ vā dadyāt, śastrapadāni vā kurvīta yady evam api na
                        gṛhṇīyāt tadā'nyāṃ grāhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.20">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.20</label>
                        <caesura/> yadā ca niviśate 'śvakhuravad ānanaṃ kṛtvonnamya ca skandhaṃ tadā
                        jānīyād gṛhṇātīti gṛhṇantīṃ cārdravastrāvacchannāṃ kṛtvā dhārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.21">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.21</label>
                        <caesura/> daṃśe toda<pc> </pc>kaṇḍu<pc> </pc>prādur<pc> </pc>bhāvair
                        jānīyāc chuddham iyam ādatta iti śuddham ādadānām apanayet atha
                        śoṇitagandhena na muñcen mukham asyāḥ saindhavacūrṇenāvakiret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.22">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.22</label>
                        <caesura/> atha patitāṃ taṇḍula<pc> </pc>kaṇḍana<pc> </pc>pradigdhagātrīṃ
                        tailalavaṇābhyaktamukhīṃ vāmahastāṅguṣṭhāṅgulībhyāṃ gṛhītapucchāṃ
                        dakṣiṇahastāṅguṣṭhāṅgulibhyāṃ śanaiḥ śanair anulomam anumārjayed ā mukhāt
                        vāmayet tāvad yāvat samyagvāntaliṅgānīti | samyagvāntā
                            salilasarake<pc> </pc>nyastā bhoktukāmā satī caret | yā sīdatī na
                        ceṣṭate sā durvāntā tāṃ punaḥ samyag vāmayet | durvāntāyā vyādhir asādhya
                        indramado nāma bhavati | atha suvāntāṃ pūrvavat sannidadhyāt || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.23">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.23</label>
                        <caesura/> śoṇitasya yogāyogān avekṣya śatadhautaghṛtābhyaṅgas tat
                        picudhāraṇaṃ vāi jalaukovraṇān madhunā'vaghaṭṭayet śitābhir adbhiś
                        pariṣecayed badhnīta vā kaṣāyamadhurasnigdhaśītaiś ca pradehaiḥ pradihyād
                        iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.24">
                        <label>1938 ed. 1.13.24</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | kṣetrāṇi grahaṇaṃ jātīḥ poṣaṇaṃ sāvacāraṇam |
                        <caesura/> jalaukasāṃ ca yo vetti tat sādhyān sa jayed gadān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.13.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne jalaukāvacāraṇīyo
                        nāma trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </l>

                <div n="14" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaḥ śoṇitavarṇanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.3</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra pāñcabhautikasya caturvidhasya ṣaḍrasasya
                        dvividhavīryasyāṣṭavidhāvīryasya vā'nekaguṇasyopayuktasyāhārasya
                        samyakpariṇatasya yas tejobhūtaḥ sāraḥ paramasūkṣmaḥ sa rasa ity ucyate
                        tasya ca hṛdayaṃ sthānaṃ sa hṛdayāc caturviṃśati dhamanīr anupraviśyor
                        dhvagā daśa daśa cādhogāminyaś catasraś ca tiryaggāḥ kṛtsnaṃ śarīram
                        aharahas tarpayati vardhayati dhārayati yāpayati cādṛṣṭahetukena karmaṇā |
                        tasya śarīram anusarato 'numānād gatir upalakṣayitavyā kṣayavṛddhivaikṛtaiḥ
                        | tasmin sarvaśarīrāvayavadoṣadhātumalāśayānusāriṇi rase jijñāsā kim ayaṃ
                        saumyas taijasa iti | atrocyate sa khalu dravānusārī
                        snehanajīvanatarpaṇadhāraṇādibhir viśeṣaiḥ saumya ity avagamyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.4</label>
                        <caesura/> sa khalv āpyo raso yakṛtplīhānau prāpya rāgam upaiti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.5</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavataś cātra | <caesura/> rañjitās tejasā tv āpaḥ śarīrasthena
                        dehinām | <caesura/> avyāpannāḥ prasannena raktam ity abhidhīyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.6</label>
                        <caesura/> rasād eva striyā raktaṃ rajaḥsaṃjñaṃ pravartate | tad varṣād
                        dvyādaśād ūrdhvaṃ yāti pañcāśataḥ kṣayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.7</label>
                        <caesura/> ārtavaṃ śoṇitaṃ tv āgneyaṃ agnīṣomīyatvād garbhasya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.8</label>
                        <caesura/> pāñcabhautikaṃ tv apare jīvaraktam āhur ācāryāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.9</label>
                        <caesura/> visratā dravatā rāgaḥ spandanaṃ laghutā tathā | <caesura/>
                        bhūmyādīnāṃ guṇā hyete dṛśyante cātra śoṇite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.10</label>
                        <caesura/> rasād raktaṃ tato māṃsaṃ māṃsān medaḥ prajāyate | <caesura/>
                        medaso 'sthi tato majjā majjñaḥ śukraṃ tu jāyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.11</label>
                        <caesura/> tatraiṣāṃ (? sarva ) dhātūnām annapānarasaḥ prīṇayitā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.12</label>
                        <caesura/> rasajaṃ puruṣaṃ vidyād rasaṃ rakṣet prayatnaḥ | annāt pānāc ca
                        matimān ācārāc cāpy atandritaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.13</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra rasa gatau dhātuḥ aharahar gacchatīty ato rasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.14</label>
                        <caesura/> sa khalu trīṇi trīṇi kalāsahasrāṇi pañcadaśa ca kalā ekaikasmin
                        dhātāv avatiṣṭhate evaṃ māsena rasaḥ śukrībhavati strīṇāṃ cārtavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.15</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> aṣṭādaśasahasrāṇi saṅkhyā hy asmin
                        samuccaye | <caesura/> kalānāṃ navatiḥ proktā svatantraparatantrayoḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.16</label>
                        <caesura/> sa śabdārcir<pc> </pc>jala<pc> </pc>santānavad aṇunā
                        viśeṣeṇānudhāvaty evaṃ śarīraṃ kevalam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.17</label>
                        <caesura/> vājīkaraṇyas tv oṣadhayaḥ svabalaguṇotkarṣād virecanavad
                        upayuktāḥ śukraṃ virecayanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.18</label>
                        <caesura/> yathā hi puṣpamukulastho gandho na śakyam ihāstīti vaktum atho
                        naivā(ā.naiva cā)stīti athavā'(? ca)sti satāṃ bhāvānām abhivyaktir iti
                        kṛ(ā.jñā)tvā kevalaṃ saukṣmyān nābhivyajyate sa eva puṣpe vivṛtapatrakeśare
                        kālāntareṇābhivyaktiṃ gacchati evaṃ bālānām api vayaḥpariṇāmāc
                        chukraprādurbhāvo bhavati romarājyādayaś ca viśeṣā nārīṇām | (? rajasi
                        copacīyamāne śanaiḥ śanaiḥ stanagarbhāśayayonyabhivṛddhir bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.19</label>
                        <caesura/> sa evānnaraso vṛddhānāṃ (? jarā)paripakvaśarīratvād aprīṇano
                        bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.20">

                        <caesura/> ta ete śrīradhāraṇād dhātava ity ucyante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.21">

                        <caesura/> teṣāṃ kṣayavṛddhī śoṇitanimitte tasmāt tad adhikṛtya vakṣyāmaḥ |
                        tatra phanilamaruṇaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ parūṣaṃ tanu śīghragamaskandi ca vātena duṣṭaṃ
                        nīlaṃ pītaṃ haritaṃ śyāvaṃ visramaniṣṭaṃ pipīlikāmakṣikāṇāmaskandi ca
                        pittaduṣṭaṃ gairikodakapratīkāśaṃ snigdhaṃ śītalaṃ bahalaṃ picchilaṃ
                        cirasrāvi māṃsapeśīprabhaṃ ca śleṣmaduṣṭaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ kāñjikābhaṃ
                        viśeṣato durgandhi ca sannipātaduṣṭaṃ (? pittavadraktenātikṛṣṇaṃ ca)
                        dvidoṣaliṅgaṃ saṃsṛṣṭaṃ | (? jīvaśoṇitamanyatra vakṣyāmaḥ )// </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.35">

                        elāśītaśivakuṣṭhatagarapāṭhābhadradāruviḍaṅgacitrakatrikaṭukāgāradhūmaharidrārkāṅkuranaktamālaphalair
                        yathālābhaṃ tribhiś caturbhiḥ samastair vā cūrṇīkṛtair lavanātailapragāḍhair
                        vraṇamukham avagharṣayed evaṃ samyak pravartate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.36">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.14.36</label>
                        <caesura/> athātipravṛtte
                        rodhramadhukapriyaṅgupattaṅgagairikasarjarasarasāñjanaśālmalīpuṣpaśaṅkhaśuktimāṣayavagodhūmacūrṇaiḥ
                        śanaiḥ śanair vraṇamukham avacūrṇyāṅgulyagreṇāvapīḍayet
                        sālasarjārjūnārimedameṣaśṛnṅgadhavadhanvantvagbhir vā cūrṇitābhiḥ kṣaumeṇa
                        vā dhmāpitena samudraphenalākṣācūrṇair vā yathoktair vraṇabandhanadravyair
                        gāḍhaṃ badhnīyāt śītāccchādanabhojanāgāraiḥ śītaiḥ pariṣekapradehaiś
                        copācaret kṣārenāgninā vā dahedyathoktaṃ vyadhanādanantaraṃ vā
                        tāmevātipravṛttāṃ sirāṃ vidhyet kākolyādikvāthaṃ vā śarkarāmadhumadhuraṃ
                        pāyayet eṇahariṇorabhraśaśamahiṣavarāhāṇāṃ vā rudhiraṃ kṣirayūṣarasaiḥ
                        susnigdhaiś cāśnīyāt upadravāṃś ca yathāsvam upacaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.37">

                        pavanaś ca paraṃ lopaṃ yāti tasmāt prayatnaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.14.38">

                        saṃdhānaṃ skandanaṃ caiva pācanaṃ dahanaṃ tathā || </l>

                            sphiggaṇḍauṣṭhopasthoruvakṣaḥ<pc> </pc>kakṣāpiṇḍikodaragrīvāśuṣkatā
