                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.24cd</label>
                        <caesura/> tadabhāvāc ca śīryante śarīrāṇi śarīriṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25abcd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.25abcd</label>
                        <caesura/> abhighātāt kṣayāt kopāc chokād dhyānāc chramāt kṣudhaḥ |
                        <caesura/> ojaḥ saṃkṣīyate hy ebhyo dhātugrahaṇaniḥsṛtam |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.25ef">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.25ef</label>
                        <caesura/> tejaḥ samīritaṃ tasmād visraṃsayate dehinaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.26-27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.26-27</label>
                        <caesura/> tasya visraṃso vyāpat kṣaya iti liṅgāni vyāpannasya bhavanti
                        sandhiviśleṣo gātrāṇāṃ sadanaṃ doṣacyavanaṃ kriyā'(O.kriyā)sannirodhaś ca
                        visraṃse stabdhagurugātratā vātaśopho varṇabhedo glānis tandrā nidrā ca
                        vyāpanne mūrcchā māṃsakṣayo mohaḥ pralāpo maraṇam iti ca kṣaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.28</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra | <caesura/> trayo doṣā balasyoktā
                        vyāpadvisraṃsanakṣayāḥ | <caesura/> viśleṣasādau gātrāṇāṃ doṣavisraṃsanaṃ
                        śramaḥ | <caesura/> aprācuryaṃ kriyānāṃ ca balavisraṃsalakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.29</label>
                        <caesura/> gurutvaṃ stabdhatā'ṇgeṣu glānirvarṇasya bhedanam | <caesura/>
                        tandrā nidrā vātaśopho balavyāpadi lakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.30</label>
                        <caesura/> mūrcchā māṃsakṣāyo mohaḥ pralāpo 'jñānam eva ca | <caesura/>
                        pūrvoktāni ca liṅgāni maraṇaṃ ca balakṣaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.31</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra visraṃse vyāpanne ca kriyāviśeṣair aviruddhair
                        balamāpyāyayet itaraṃ tu mūḍhasaṃjñaṃ varjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.32</label>
                        <caesura/> doṣadhātumalakṣīṇo balakṣīṇi'pi vā naraḥ | <caesura/>
                        svayonivardhanaṃ yattadannapānaṃ prakāṅkṣati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.33">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.33</label>
                        <caesura/> yadyadāhārajātaṃ tu kṣīṇaḥ prārthayate naraḥ | <caesura/> tasya
                        tasya sa lābhe tu taṃ taṃ kṣayamapohati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.34">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.34</label>
                        <caesura/> yasya dhātukṣayād vāyuḥ saṃjñāṃ karma ca nāśayet | <caesura/>
                        prakṣiṇaṃ ca balaṃ yasya nāsu śakyaś cikitsitum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.35">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.35</label>
                        <caesura/> rasanimittam eva sthaulyaṃ kārśyaṃ ca | tatra śleṣmalāhārasevino
                        'dhyaśanaśīlasyāvyāyāmino divāsvapnaratasya cāma evānnaraso madhurataraś ca
                        śarīram anukrāmann atisnehān medo janayati tad atisthaulyam āpādayati tam
                        atisthūlaṃ
                        kṣudraśvāsapipāsākṣutsvapnasvedagātradaurgandhyakrathanagātrasādagadgadatvāni
                        kṣipram evāviśanti saukumāryān medasaḥ sarvakriyāsvasamarthaḥ kaphamedo
                        niruddhamārgartvāc cālpavyavāyo bhavati āvṛtamārgatvād eva śeṣā dhātavo
                        nāpyāyante 'tyarthamato 'lpaprāṇo bhavati
                        pramehapīḍakājvarabhagandaravidradhivātavikārāṇāmanyataṃ prāpya pañcatvam
                        upayāti sarva eva cāsya rogā balavanto bhavanty āvṛtamārgatvāt srotasāṃ atas
                        tasyotpattihetuṃ pariharet | utpanne tu
                        śilājatuguggulugomūtratriphalāloharajorasāñjanamadhuyavamudgakoradūṣakaśyāmākoddālakādīnāṃ
                        virūkṣaṇacchedanīyānāṃ dravyāṇaṃ vidhivad upayogo vyāyāmo
                        lekhanabastyupayogaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.36">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.36</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra punar vātalāhārasevino
                        'tivyāyāmavyavāyādhyayanabhayaśokadhyānarātrijāgaraṇapipāsākṣutkaṣāyālpāśanaprabhṛtibhir
                        upaśoṣito rasadhātuḥ śarīram ananukrāman nalpatvān na prīṇāti tasmād
                        atikārśyaṃ bhavati so 'tikṛśaḥ kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇavātavarṣabhārādāneṣv
                        asahiṣṇur vātarogaprāyo 'lpaprāṇaś ca kriyāsu bhavati
                        śvāsakāsaśoṣaplīhodarāgnisādagulmaraktapittānām anyatamam āsādya maraṇam
                        upayāti sarva eva cāsya rogā balavanto bhavanty alpaprāṇatvāt atas
                        tasyotpattihetuṃ pariharet | utpanne tu
                        payasyāśvagandhāvidārigandhāśatāvarībalātibalānāgabalānāṃ madhurāṇām anyāsaṃ
                        cauṣadhīnām upayogaḥ kṣīradadhighṛtamāṃsaśāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmānāṃ ca
                        divāsvapnabrahmacaryāvyāyāmabṛhaṇabastyupayogaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.37</label>
                        <caesura/> yaḥ punar ubhayasādhāraṇāny āseveta tasyān narasaḥ śarīram
                        anukrāman samān dhātūn upacinoti samadhātutvān madhyaśarīro bhavati
                        sarvakriyāsu samarthaḥ kṣutpipāsāśītoṣṇavarṣātapasaho balavāṃś ca sa satatam
                        anupālayitavya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.38">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.38</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra | <caesura/> atyantagarhitāv etau sadā sthūlakṛśau
                        narau | <caesura/> śreṣṭho madhyaśarīras tu kṛśaḥ sthūlāt tu pūjitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.39">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.39</label>
                        <caesura/> doṣaḥ prakupito dhātūn kṣapayaty ātmatejasā | <caesura/> iddhaḥ
                        svatejasā vahnir ukhāgatam ivodakam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.40">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.40</label>
                        <caesura/> vailakṣaṇyāc charīrāṇām asthāyitvāt tathaiva ca | <caesura/>
                        doṣadhātumalānāṃ tu parimāṇaṃ na vidyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.41">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.41</label>
                        <caesura/> eṣāṃ samatvaṃ yac cāpi bhiṣagbhir avadhāryate | <caesura/> na tat
                        svāsthyādṛte śakyaṃ vaktum anyena hetunā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.42">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.42</label>
                        <caesura/> doṣādīnāṃ tv asamatām anumānena lakṣayet | <caesura/>
                        aprasannendriyaṃ vīkṣya puruṣaṃ kuśalo bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.43</label>
                        <caesura/> svasthasya rakṣaṇaṃ kuryād asvasthasya tu buddhimān | <caesura/>
                        kṣapayed bṛṃhayec cāpi doṣadhātumalān bhiṣak | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.43ef">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.43ef</label>
                        <caesura/> tāvad yāvad arogaḥ syād etat sāmyasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.15.44">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.15.44</label>
                        <caesura/> samadoṣaḥ samāgniś ca samadhātumalakriyaḥ | <caesura/>
                        prasannātmendriyamanāḥ svasthā ity abhidhīyate ||</l>

                    <head>ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaḥ karṇavyadha<pc> </pc>bandha<pc> </pc>vidhim adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanavatariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.3</label>
                        <caesura/> rakṣābhūṣaṇanimittaṃ bālasya karṇau vidhyete | tau ṣaṣṭhe māsi
                        saptame vā śuklapakṣe praśasteṣu tithikaraṇamuhūrtanakṣatreṣu
                        kṛtamaṅgalasvastivācanaṃ dhātryaṅke kumāradharāṅke vā kumāram upaveśya
                        bālakrīḍanakaiḥ pralobhyābhisāntvayan bhiṣag vāmahastenākṛṣya karṇaṃ
                        daivakṛte chidra ādityakarāvabhāsite śanaiḥ śanair dakṣiṇahastena rju
                        vidhyet pratanukaṃ sūcyā bahalam ārayā pūrvaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ kumārasya vāmaṃ
                        kumāryāḥ tataḥ picuvartiṃ praveśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.4</label>
                        <caesura/> śoṇita<pc> </pc>bahutvena vedanayā cānyadeśaviddham iti jānīyāt
                        nirupadravatayā taddeśaviddham iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.5</label>
                        <caesura/> tatrājñena yadṛcchayā viddhāsu sirāsu
                        kālikāmarmarikālohitikāsūpadravā bhavanti | tatra kālikāyāṃ jvaro dāhaḥ
                        śvayathur vedanā ca bhavati marmarikāyāṃ vedanā jvaro granthayaś ca
                        lohitikāyāṃ manyāstambhāpatānakaśirograhakarṇaśūlāni bhavanti | teṣu
                        yathāsvaṃ pratikurvīta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.6</label>
                        <caesura/> kliṣṭajihmāpraśastasūcīvyadhād gāḍhataravartitvād doṣasamudāyād
                        apraśastavyadhād vā yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra vartim
                        upahṛtyāśu madhukairaṇḍa<pc> </pc>mūla<pc> </pc>mañjiṣṭhā<pc
                            > </pc>yava<pc> </pc>tila<pc> </pc>kalkair madhughṛtapragāḍhair ālepayet
                        tāvad yāvat surūḍha iti surūḍhaṃ cainaṃ punar vidhyet vidhānaṃ tu pūrvoktam
                        eva || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.7</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra samyagviddham āmatailena pariṣecayet tryahāt tryahāc ca
                        vartiṃ sthūlatarāṃ dadyāt pariṣekaṃ ca tam eva || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.8</label>
                        <caesura/> atha vyapagatadoṣopadrave karṇe vardhanārthaṃ laghuvardhanakaṃ
                        kuryāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.9</label>
                        <caesura/> evaṃ vivardhitaḥ karṇaś chidyate tu dvidhā nṛṇām | <caesura/>
                        doṣato vā'bhighātād vā sandhānaṃ tasya me śṛṇu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.10</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra samāsena pañcadaśakarṇabandhākṛtayaḥ | tad yathā
                        nemisandhānaka utpalabhedyako vallūraka āsaṅgimo gaṇḍakarṇa āhāryo
                        nirvedhimo vyāyojimaḥ kapāṭasandhiko 'rdhakapāṭasandhikaḥ saṃkṣipto
                        hīnakarṇo vallīkarṇo yaṣṭikarṇaḥ kākauṣṭhaka iti | teṣu
                        pṛthulāyatasamobhayapālir nemisandhānakaḥ vṛttāyatasamobhayapālir
                        utpalabhedyakaḥ hrasvavṛttasamobhayapālir vallūrakaḥ
                        abhyantaradīrghaikapālir āsaṅgimaḥ bāhya<pc> </pc>dīrghaikapālir gaṇḍakarṇaḥ
                        | apālir ubhayato 'py āhāryaḥ pīṭhopamapālir ubhayataḥ kṣīṇaputrikāśrito
                        nirvedhimaḥ | sthūlāṇusamaviṣamapālir vyāyojimaḥ | abhyantaradīrghaikapālir
                        itarālpapāliḥ | kapāṭasandhikaḥ bāhyadīrghaikapālir itarālpapālir
                        ardhakapāṭasandhikaḥ | tatra daśaite karṇabandhavikalpāḥ sādhyāḥ teṣāṃ
                        svanāmabhir evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyākhyātāḥ | saṃkṣiptādayaḥ pañcāsādhyāḥ |
                        tatra śuṣkaśaṣkulir utsannapālir itarālpapāliḥ saṃkṣiptaḥ anadhiṣṭhānapāliḥ
                        paryantayoḥ kṣīṇamāṃso hīnakarṇaḥ tanuviṣamālpapālir vallīkarṇaḥ
                        grathitamāṃsastabdhasirāsaṃtatasūkṣmapālir yaṣṭikarṇaḥ
                        nirmāṃsasaṃkṣiptāgrālpaśoṇitapāliḥ kākauṣṭhaka iti | baddheṣv api tu
                            śopha<pc> </pc>dāha<pc> </pc>rāga<pc> </pc>pāka<pc
                            > </pc>piḍakā<pc> </pc>srāva<pc> </pc>yuktā na siddhim upayānti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.11</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra | <caesura/> yasya pālidvayam api karṇasya na
                        bhaved iha | <caesura/> karṇapīṭhaṃ same madhye tasya viddhvā vivardhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.12</label>
                        <caesura/> bāhyāyām iha dīrghāyāṃ sandhir ābhyantaro bhavet | <caesura/>
                        ābhyantarāyāṃ dīrghāyāṃ bāhyasandhir udāhṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.13</label>
                        <caesura/> ekaiva tu bhavet pāliḥ sthūlā pṛthvī sthirā ca yā | <caesura/>
                        tāṃ dvidhā pāṭayitvā tu chittvā copari sandhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.14</label>
                        <caesura/> gaṇḍād utpāṭya māṃsena sānubandhena jīvatā | <caesura/>
                        karṇapālīm āpāles tu kuryān nirlikhya śāstravit || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.15</label>
                        <caesura/> ato nyatamaṃ bandhaṃ cikīrṣur
                        agropaharaṇīyoktopasaṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraṃ viśeṣataś cātropaharet surāmaṇḍaṃ
                        kṣīram udakaṃ dhānyāmlaṃ kapālacūrṇaṃ ceti | tato 'ṅganāṃ puruṣaṃ vā
                        grathitakeśāntaṃ laghubhuktavantam āptaiḥ suparigṛhītaṃ ca kṛtvā bandham
                        upadhārya chedyabhedyalekhyavyadhanair upapannair upapādya karṇaśoṇitam
                        avekṣya duṣṭam aduṣṭaṃ veti tatra vātaduṣṭe dhānyāmloṣṇodakābhyāṃ pittaduṣṭe
                        śītodakapayobhyāṃ śleṣmaduṣṭe surāmaṇḍoṣṇodakābhyāṃ prakṣālya karṇau punar
                        avalikhyānunnatam ahīnam aviṣamaṃ ca karṇasandhiṃ sanniveśya sthitaraktaṃ
                        sandadhyāt | tato madhughṛtenābhyajya picuprotayor anyatareṇāvaguṇṭhya
                        sūtreṇānavagāḍhaman atiśithilaṃ ca baddhvā kapālacūrṇenāvakīryācārikam
                        upadiśed dvivraṇīyoktena ca vidhānenopacaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.16</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16x">

                        <caesura/> vighaṭṭanaṃ divāsvapnaṃ vyāyāmam atibhojanam | <caesura/>
                        vyavāyam agnisaṃtāpaṃ vākśramaṃ ca vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.16.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.16.1</label>
                        <caesura/> (?āmatailaparīṣekaṃ trirātramavacārayet | <caesura/> tatas

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.17">

                        <caesura/> na cāśuddharaktam atipravṛttaraktaṃ kṣīṇaraktaṃ vā saṃdadhyāt |
                        sa hi vātaduṣṭe rakte rūḍho 'pi paripuṭanavān pittaduṣṭe
                        dāhapākarāgavedanāvān śleṣmaduṣṭe stabdhaḥ kaṇḍūmān atipravṛttarakte
                        śyāvaśophavān kṣīṇo 'lpamāṃso na vṛddhim upaiti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.18</label>
                        <caesura/> āmatailena trirātraṃ pariṣecayet trirātrāc ca picuṃ parivartayet
                        | sa yadā surūḍho nirupadravaḥ savarṇo bhavati tadainaṃ śanaiś śanair
                        abhivardhayet | ato 'nyathā saṃrambhadāhapākarāgavedanāvān punaś chidyate vā
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.19</label>
                        <caesura/> athāsyāpraduṣṭasyābhivardhanārtham abhyaṅgaḥ | tad yathā
                        godhāpratudaviṣkirānūpaudakavasāmajjānau payaḥ sarpis tailaṃ gaurasarṣapajaṃ
                        ca yathālābhaṃ
                        saṃbhṛtyārkālarkabalātibalānantāpāmārgāśvagandhāvidārigandhākṣīraśuklājalaśūkamadhuravargapayasyāprativāpaṃ
                        tailaṃ vā pācayitvā svanuguptaṃ nidadhyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.20</label>
                        <caesura/> sveditonmarditaṃ karṇaṃ snehenaitena yojayet | <caesura/> ato
                        'nupadravaḥ samyag balavāṃś ca vivardhate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.21</label>
                        <caesura/> yavāśvagandhāyaṣṭyāhvais tilaiś codvartanaṃ hitam | <caesura/>
                        śatāvaryaśvagandhābhyāṃ payasyair aṇḍajīvanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.22</label>
                        <caesura/> tailaṃ vipakvaṃ sakṣīram abhyaṅgāt pālivardhanam | <caesura/> ye
                        tu karṇā na vardhante svedasnehopapāditāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.23</label>
                        <caesura/> teṣām apāṅgadeśe tu kuryāt pracchānam eva tu |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.23b">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.23b</label>
                        <caesura/> bāhyacchedaṃ na kurvīta vyāpadaḥ syus tato dhruvāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.24</label>
                        <caesura/> baddhamātraṃ tu yaḥ karṇaṃ sahasaivābhivardhayet | <caesura/>
                        āmakośī samādhmātaḥ kṣipram eva vimucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.25</label>
                        <caesura/> jātaromā suvartmā ca śliṣṭasandhiḥ samaḥ sthiraḥ | <caesura/>
                        surūḍho 'vedano yaś ca taṃ karṇaṃ vardhayec chanaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.0">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.0</label>
                        <caesura/> amitāḥ karṇabandhās tu vijñeyāḥ kuśalair iha | <caesura/> yo
                        yathā suviśiṣṭaḥ syāt taṃ tathā viniyojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.1</label>
                        <caesura/> (karṇapālyāmayān nṝṇāṃ punar vakṣyāmi suśruta | <caesura/>
                        karṇapalyāṃ prakupaitā vātapittakaphās trayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.2</label>
                        <caesura/> dvidhā vāpy atha saṃsṛṣṭāḥ kurvanti vividhā rujaḥ | <caesura/>
                        visphoṭaḥ stabdhatā śophaḥ pālyāṃ doṣe tu vātike || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.3</label>
                        <caesura/> dāhavisphoṭajananaṃ śophaḥ pākaś ca paittike | <caesura/> kaṇḍūḥ
                        saśvayathuḥ stambho gurutvaṃ ca kaphātmake || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.4</label>
                        <caesura/> yathādoṣaṃ ca saṃśodhya kuryāt teṣāṃ cikitsitam | <caesura/>
                        svedābhyaṅgaparīṣekaiḥ pralepāsṛgvimokṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.5</label>
                        <caesura/> mṛdvīṃ kriyāṃ bṛṃhaṇīyair yathāsvaṃ bhojanais tathā | <caesura/>
                        ya evaṃ vetti doṣāṇāṃ cikitsāṃ kartum arhati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.6</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ nāmaliṅgair vakṣye pālyām upadravān | <caesura/>
                        atpāṭakaś cotpuṭakaḥ śyāvaḥ kaṇḍūyuto bhṛśam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.7</label>
                        <caesura/> avamanthaḥ sakaṇḍūko granthiko jambulas tathā | <caesura/> srāvī
                        ca dāhavāṃś caiva śṛṇveṣāṃ kramaśaḥ kriyām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.8</label>
                        <caesura/> apāmārgaḥ sarjarasaḥ pāṭalālakucatvacau | <caesura/> utpāṭake
                        pralepaḥ syāt tailam ebhiś ca pācayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.9</label>
                        <caesura/> śampākaśigrupūtīkān godhāmedo 'tha tadvasām | <caesura/> vārāhaṃ
                        gavyam aiṇeyaṃ pittaṃ sarpiś ca saṃsṛjet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.10</label>
                        <caesura/> lepam utpuṭake dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam | <caesura/>
                        gaurīṃ sugandhāṃ saśyāmām anantāṃ taṇḍulīyakam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.11</label>
                        <caesura/> śyāve pralepanaṃ dadyāt tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam | <caesura/>
                        pāṭhāṃ rasāñjanaṃ kṣaudraṃ tathā syād uṣṇakāñjikam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.12</label>
                        <caesura/> dadyāl lepaṃ sakaṇḍūke tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam | <caesura/>
                        vraṇībhūtasya deyaṃ syād idaṃ tailaṃ vijānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.13</label>
                        <caesura/> madhukakṣīrakākolījīvakādyair vipācitam | <caesura/>
                        godhāvarāhasarpāṇāṃ vasāḥ syuḥ kṛtabṛṃhaṇe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.14</label>
                        <caesura/> pralepanam idaṃ dadyād avasicyāvamanthake | <caesura/>
                        prapauṇḍarīkaṃ madhukaṃ samaṅgāṃ dhavam eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.15</label>
                        <caesura/> tailam ebhiś ca saṃpakvaṃ śṛṇu kaṇḍūmataḥ kriyām | <caesura/>
                        sahadevā viśvadevā ajākṣīraṃ sasaindhavam | <caesura/> etair ālepanaṃ dadyāt
                        tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.16</label>
                        <caesura/> granthike guṭikāṃ pūrvaṃ srāvayed avapāṭya tu | <caesura/> tataḥ
                        saindhavacūrṇaṃ tu ghṛṣṭvā lepaṃ pradāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.17</label>
                        <caesura/> likhitvā tatsrutaṃ ghṛṣṭvā cūrṇair lodhrasya jambule | <caesura/>
                        kṣīreṇa pratisāryainaṃ śuddhaṃ saṃropayet tataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.18</label>
                        <caesura/> madhuparṇī madhūkaṃ ca ma madhukaṃ madhunā saha | <caesura/>
                        lepaḥ srāviṇi dātavyas tailam ebhiś ca sādhitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.26.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.26.19</label>
                        <caesura/> pañcavalkaiḥ samadhukaiḥ piṣṭais taiś ca ghṛtānvitaiḥ |
                        <caesura/> jīvakādyaiḥ sasarpiṣkair dahyamānaṃ pralepayet ||) </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.27</label>
                        <caesura/> viśleṣitāyās tv atha nāsikāyā <caesura/> vakṣyāmi sandhānavidhiṃ
                        yathāvat | <caesura/> nāsāpramāṇaṃ pṛthivīruhāṇāṃ <caesura/> patraṃ gṛhītvā
                        tv avalambi tasya || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.28</label>
                        <caesura/> tena pramāṇena hi gaṇḍapārśvād <caesura/> utkṛtya baddhaṃ tv atha
                        nāsikāgram | <caesura/> vilikhya cāśu pratisaṃdadhīta <caesura/> tat
                        sādhubandhair bhiṣag apramattaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.29</label>
                        <caesura/> susaṃhitaṃ samyag ato yathāvan <caesura/> nāḍīdvayenābhisamīkṣya
                        baddhvā | <caesura/> pronnamya cainām avacūrṇayet tu <caesura/>
                        pataṅgayaṣṭīmadhukāñjanaiś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.30</label>
                        <caesura/> saṃchādya samyak picunā sitena <caesura/> tailena siñced asakṛt
                        tilānām | <caesura/> ghṛtaṃ ca pāyyaḥ sa naraḥ sujīrṇe <caesura/> snigdho
                        virecyaḥ sa yathopadeśam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.31</label>
                        <caesura/> rūḍhaṃ ca sandhānam upāgataṃ syāt <caesura/> tad ardhaśeṣaṃ tu
                        punar nikṛntet | <caesura/> hīnāṃ punar vardhayituṃ yateta <caesura/> samāṃ
                        ca kuryād ativṛddhamāṃsām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.16.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.16.32</label>
                        <caesura/> nāḍīyogaṃ vinauṣṭhasya nāsāsandhānavad vidhim | <caesura/> ya
                        evam eva jānīyāt sa rājñaḥ kartum arhati || </l>

                    <trailer xml:id="SS.1.16.colophon">iti śrīsuśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        karṇavyadhabandhavidhirnāma ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </trailer>

                <div n="17" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāta āmapakvaiṣaṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.3</label>
                        <caesura/> śophasamutthānā granthividradhyalajīprabhṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa vyādhayo
                        'bhihitā anekākṛtayaḥ tair vilakṣaṇaḥ pṛthurgrathitaḥ samo viṣamo vā
                        tvaṅnāṃsasthāyī doṣasaṃghātaḥ śarīraikadeśotthitaḥ śopha ity ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.4</label>
                        <caesura/> sa ṣaḍvidho vātapittakaphaśoṇitasannipātāgantunimittaḥ | tasya
                        doṣarūpavyañjanair lakṣaṇāni vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | tatra vātaśopho 'ruṇaḥ kṛṣṇo vā
                        paruṣo mṛduranavasthitāstodāyaś cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti pittaśophaḥ pīto
                        mṛduḥ sarakto vā śīghrānusāryoṣādayaś cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti
                        śleṣmaśophaḥ pāṇḍuḥ śuklo vā kaṭhinaḥ śitaḥ snigdho mandānusārī kaṇḍvādayaś
                        cātra vedanāviśeṣā bhavanti sarvavarṇavedanaḥ sannipātajaḥ pittavacchoṇitajo
                        'tikṛṣṇaś ca pittaraktalakṣaṇa āganturlohitāvabhāsaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.5</label>
                        <caesura/> sa yadā bāhyābhyantaraiḥ kriyāviśeṣair na saṃbhāvitaḥ
                        praśamayituṃ kriyāviparyayādbahutvād vā doṣāṇāṃ tadā pākābhimukho bhavati |
                        tasyāmsya pacyamānasya pakvasya ca lakṣaṇamucyamānam upadhāraya | tatra
                        mandoṣmatā tvaksavarṇatā śītaśophatā sthairyaṃ mandavedanatā'lpaśophatā
                        cāmalakṣaṇamuddiṣṭaṃ sūcibhir iva nistudyate daśyata iva pipīlikābhis tābhiś
                        ca saṃsarpyata iva chidyata iva śastreṇa bhidyata iva śaktibhis tāḍyata iva
                        daṇḍena pīḍyata iva pāṇinā ghaṭyata iva cāṅgulyā dahyate pacyata iva
                        cāgnikṣārābhyāṃ oṣacoṣaparīdāhāś ca bhavanti vṛś cikaviddha iva ca
                        sthānāsanaśayaneṣu na śāntim upaiti ādhmātabastirivātataś ca śopho bhavati
                        tvagvaivarṇyaṃ śophābhivṛddhirjvaradāhapipāsā bhaktāruciś ca pacyamānaliṅgaṃ
                        vedanopaśāntiḥ pāṇḍutā'lpaśophatā valīprādurbhāvastvakparipuṭanaṃ
                        nimnadarśanamaṅgulyā'vapīḍite pratyunnamanaṃ bastāvivodakasaṃcaraṇaṃ pūyasya
                        prapīḍayatyekamantamante vā'vapīḍite muhurmuhustodaḥ kaṇḍūrunnatatā vyādher
                        upadravaśāntirbhaktābhikāṅkṣā ca pakvaliṅgam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.6</label>
                        <caesura/> kaphajeṣu tu rogeṣu gambhīragatitvād abhighātajeṣu vā keṣucid
                        asamastaṃ pakvalakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā pakvam apakvam iti manyamāno bhiṣaṅnoham
                        upaiti | yatra hi tvaksavarṇatā śītaśophatā sthaulyamalparujatā'śmavac ca
                        ghanatā na tatra moham upeyād iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.7</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra | <caesura/> āmaṃ vipacyamānaṃ ca samyak pakvaṃ ca
                        yo bhiṣak | <caesura/> jānīyāt sa bhaved vaidyaḥ śeṣās taskaravṛttayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.8</label>
                        <caesura/> vātādṛte nāsti rujā na pākaḥ pittādṛte nāsti kaphāc ca pūyaḥ |
                        <caesura/> tasmāt samastāḥ paripākakāle pacanti śophāṃs traya eva doṣāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.9</label>
                        <caesura/> kālāntareṇābhyuditaṃ tu pittaṃ kṛtvā vaśe vātakaphau prasahya |
                        <caesura/> pacaty ataḥ śoṇitam eva pāko mato 'pareṣāṃ viduṣāṃ dvitīyaḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.10</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra āmacchede māṃsasirāsnāyvasthisandhivyāpādanam atimātraṃ
                        śoṇitātipravṛttir vedanāprādurbhāvo 'vadaraṇam anekopadravadarśanaṃ
                        kṣatavidradhirvā bhavati | sa yadā bhayamohābhyāṃ pakvam apy apakvam iti
                        manyamānaś ciram upekṣate vyādhiṃ vaidyas tadā gambhīrānugato dvāram
                        alabhamānaḥ pūyaḥ svam āśrayam avadā(ā.dī)ryotasaṅgaṃ mahāntam avakāśaṃ
                        kṛtvā nāḍīṃ janayitvā kṛcchrasādhyo bhavaty asādhyo veti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.11</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra | <caesura/> yaś chinatty āmam ajñānād yaś ca
                        pakvam upekṣate | <caesura/> śvapacāv iva mantavyau tāv aniścitakāriṇau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.12</label>
                        <caesura/> prāk śastrakarmaṇaś ceṣṭaṃ bhojayed āturaṃ bhiṣak | <caesura/>
                        madyapaṃ pāyayen madyaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ yo vedanāsahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.13</label>
                        <caesura/> na mūrcchaty annasaṃyogān mattaḥ śastraṃ na budhyate | <caesura/>
                        tasmād avaśyaṃ bhoktavyaṃ rogeṣūkteṣu karmaṇi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.14</label>
                        <caesura/> prāṇo hy ābhyantaro nṇṇāṃ bāhyaprāṇaguṇānvitaḥ | <caesura/>
                        dhārayaty avirodhena śarīraṃ pāñcabhautikam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.15</label>
                        <caesura/> alpo mahān vā kriyayā vinā yaḥ samucchritaḥ pākam upaiti śophaḥ |
                        <caesura/> viśālamūlo viṣamo vidagdhaḥ sa kṛcchritāṃ yāty avagāḍhadoṣaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.16</label>
                        <caesura/> ālepavisrāvaṇaśodhanais tu samyak prayukair yadi nopaśāmyet |
                        <caesura/> pacyet śīghraṃ samam alpamūlaḥ sa piṇḍitaś copari connataḥ syāt
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.17</label>
                        <caesura/> kakṣaṃ samāsādya yathaiva vahnir vāte(ā.yvī)ritaḥ saṃdahati
                        prasahya | <caesura/> tathaiva pūyo 'py aviniḥsṛto hi māṃsaṃ sirāḥ snāyu ca
                        khādatīha || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.18</label>
                        <caesura/> ādau vimlāpanaṃ kuryād dvitīyam avasecanam | <caesura/> tṛtīyam
                        upanāhaṃ tu caturthīṃ pāṭanakriyām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.19</label>
                        <caesura/> pañcamaṃ śodhanaṃ kuryāt ṣaṣṭhaṃ ropaṇam iṣyate | <caesura/> ete
                        kramā vraṇasyoktāḥ saptamaṃ vaikṛtāpaham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.17.trailer">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.17.trailer</label>
                        <caesura/> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne āmapakvaiṣaṇīyo 'nāma saptadaśo
                        'dhyāyaḥ || </l>
                </div>


                <div n="18" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>aṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāto vraṇālepanabandhavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.3</label>
                        <caesura/> ālipa ādya upakramaḥ eṣa sarvaśophānāṃ sāmānyaḥ pradhānatamaś ca
                        taṃ ca pratirogaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tato bandhaḥ pradhānaṃ tena
                        śuddhirvraṇaropaṇamasthisaṃdhisthairyaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.4</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra pratilomamālimpennānulomam | pratilome hi
                        samyagauṣadhamavatiṣṭhate 'nupraviśati romakūpān svedavāhibhiś ca
                        sirāmukhairvīryaṃ prāpnoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.5</label>
                        <caesura/> na ca śuṣyamāṇamupekṣeta anyatra pīḍayitavyāt śuṣko hy apārthako
                        rukkaraś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.6</label>
                        <caesura/> sa trividhaḥ pralepaḥ pradeha ālepaś ca | teṣām antaraṃ pralepaḥ
                        śītas tanur aviśoṣī viśoṣī ca pradehas tūṣṇaḥ śīto vā bahalo 'bahur aviśoṣī
                        ca madhaymo 'trālepaḥ | tatra raktapittaprasādakṛd ālepaḥ pradeho
                        vātaśleṣmapraśamanaḥ saṃdhānaḥ śodhano ropaṇaḥ śophavedanāpahaś ca
                        tasyopayogaḥ kṣatākṣateṣu yas tu kṣateṣūpayujyate sa bhūyaḥ kalka iti
                        saṃjñāṃ labhate niruddālepanasaṃjñaḥ tenāsrāvasannirodho mṛdutā
                        pūtimāṃsāpakarṣaṇam anantardoṣatā vraṇaśuddhiś ca bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.7</label>
                        <caesura/> avidagdheṣu śopheṣu hitam ālepanaṃ bhavet | <caesura/> yathāsvaṃ
                        doṣaśamanaṃ dāhakaṇḍūrujāpaham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.8</label>
                        <caesura/> tvakprasādanam evāgryaṃ māṃsaraktaprasādanam | <caesura/>
                        dāhapraśamanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ todakaṇḍūvināśanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.9</label>
                        <caesura/> marmadeśeṣu ye togā guhyeṣv api tathā nṛām | <caesura/>
                        saṃśodhanāya teṣāṃ hi kuryād ālepanaṃ bhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.10</label>
                        <caesura/> (?ṣaḍbhāgaṃ paittike snehaṃ catrubhāgaṃ tu vātike | <caesura/>
                        aṣṭabhāgaṃ tu kaphaje snehamātrāṃ pradāpayet ||) </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.11</label>
                        <caesura/> tasya pramāṇamārdramāhiṣacarmotsedham upadiśanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.12</label>
                        <caesura/> na cālepaṃ rātrau prayuñjīta mābhūc chaityapihitoṣmaṇas tad
                        anirgamād vikārapravṛtti(ā.ddhi)r iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.13</label>
                        <caesura/> pradehasādhye vyādhau tu hitam ālepanaṃ divā | <caesura/>
                        pittaraktābhighātotthe saviṣe ca viśeṣataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.14</label>
                        <caesura/> na ca paryuṣitaṃ lepaṃ kadācidavacārayet | <caesura/> upary upari
                        lepaṃ tu na kadācit pradāpayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.15</label>
                        <caesura/> ūṣmāṇaṃ vedanāṃ dāhaṃ ghanatvājjanayet sa hi | <caesura/> na ca
                        tenaiva lepena pradehaṃ dāpayet punaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.15ef">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.15ef</label>
                        <caesura/> śuṣkabhāvāt sa nirvīryo yukto 'pi syād apārthakaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.16</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ vraṇabandhanadravyāṇy upadekṣyāmaḥ tad yathā
                        kṣaumakārpāsāvikadukūlakauśeyapatrorṇacīnapaṭṭacarmāntarvalkalālābūśakalalatāvidalarajjutūlaphalasantānikālauhānīti
                        teṣaṃ vyādhiṃ kālaṃ cāvekṣyopayogaḥ prakaraṇataś caiṣām ādeśaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.17</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra
                        kośadāmasvastikānuvellitapra(ā.mu)tolīmaṇḍalasthagikāyamakakhaṭvācīnavibandhavitānagophaṇāḥ
                        pañcāṅgī ceti caturdaśa bandhaviśeṣāḥ | teṣāṃ nāmabhir evākṛtayaḥ prāyeṇa
                        vyākhyātāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.18</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra kośamaṅguṣṭhāṅguliparvasu vidadhyāt dāmasaṃbādhe 'ṅge
                        sandhikūrcakabhrūstanāntaratalakarṇeṣu svastikaṃ anuvellitaṃ tu śākhāsu
                        grīvāmeḍhrayoḥ pratolīṃ vṛtte 'ṅge maṇḍalaṃ aṅguṣṭhāṅgulimeḍhrāgreṣu
                        sthagikāṃ yamalavraṇayor yamakaṃ hanuśaṅkhagaṇḍeṣu khaṭvāṃ apāṅgayoś cīnaṃ
                        pṛṣṭhodaroraḥsu vibandhaṃ mūrdhani vitānaṃ cibukanāsauṣṭhāṃsabastiṣu
                        gophaṇāṃ jatruṇa ūrdhvaṃ pañcāṅgīm iti yo vā yasmin śarīrapradeśe suniviṣṭo
                        bhavati taṃ tasmin vidadhyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.19</label>
                        <caesura/> yantraṇam ūrdhvamadhistiryak ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.20</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra ghanāṃ kavalikāṃ dattvā vāmahastaparikṣepamṛjum anāviddham
                        asaṃkucitaṃ mṛdu paṭṭaṃ niveśya badhnīyāt | na ca vraṇasyopari kuryād
                        granthim ābādhakaraṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.21</label>
                        <caesura/> na ca vikeśikauṣadhe 'tisnigdhe 'tirūkṣe viṣame vā kurvīta yasmād
                        atisnehāt kledo raukṣyāc chedo durnyāsāhraṇavartmāvagharṣaṇam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.22</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra vraṇayatanaviśeṣād bandhaviśeṣas trividho bhavati gāḍhaḥ
                        samaḥ śithila iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.23</label>
                        <caesura/> pīḍayann arujo gāḍhaḥ socchvāsaḥ śithilaḥ smṛtaḥ | <caesura/>
                        naiva gāḍho na śithilaḥ samo bandhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.24</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra sphikkukṣikakṣāvaṅkṣaṇoruśiraḥsu gāḍhaḥ
                        śākhāvadanakarṇakaṇṭhameḍhramuṣkapṛṣṭhapārśvodaroraḥsu samaḥ akṣṇoḥ sandhiṣu
                        ca śithila ti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.25</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra paittikaṃ gāḍhasthāne samaṃ badhnīyāt samasthāne śithilaṃ
                        śithilasthāne naiva evaṃ śoṇitaduṣṭaṃ ca ślaiṣmikaṃ śithilasthāne samaṃ
                        samasthāne gāḍhaṃ gāḍhasthāne gāḍhataraṃ evaṃ vātaduṣṭaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.26">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.26</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra paittikaṃ śaradi grīṣme dvirahno badhnīyāt
                        raktopadrutamapyevaṃ ślaiṣmikaṃ hemantavasantayostryahāt vātopadrutamapyevam
                        | evamabhyūhya bandhaviparyayaṃ ca kuryāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.27</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra samaśithilasthāneṣu gāḍhaṃ baddhe vikeśikauṣadhanair
                        arthakyaṃ śophavedanāprādurbhāvaś ca gāḍhasamasthāneṣu śithilaṃ baddhe
                        vikeśikauṣadhapatanaṃ paṭṭasaṃcārāhraṇavartmāvagharṣanam iti
                        gāḍhaśithilasthāneṣu samaṃ baddhe ca guṇābhāva iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.28</label>
                        <caesura/> aviparītabandhe vedanopaśāntir asṛkprasādo mārdavaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.29</label>
                        <caesura/> abadhyamāno
                        daṃśamaśakatṛṇakāṣṭhopalapāṃśuśītavātātapaprabhṛtibhir viśeṣair abhihanyate
                        vraṇo vividhavedanopadrutaś ca duṣṭatām upaity ālepanādīni cāsya viśoṣam
                        upayānti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.30</label>
                        <caesura/> cūrṇitaṃ mathitaṃ bhagnaṃ viśliṣṭam atipātitam | <caesura/>
                        asthisnāyusirācchinnam āśu bandhena rohati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.31</label>
                        <caesura/> sukham evaṃ vraṇī śete sukhaṃ gacchati tiṣṭhati | <caesura/>
                        sukhaṃ śayyāsanasthasya kṣipraṃ saṃrohati vraṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.32</label>
                        <caesura/> abandhyāḥ pittaraktābhighātaviṣanimittā yadā ca
                        śophadāhapākarāgatodavedanābhibhūtāḥ kṣārāgnidagdhāḥ pākāt
                        prakuthitapraśīrṇamāṃsāś ca bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.33">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.33</label>
                        <caesura/> kuṣṭhinām agnidagdhānāṃ piḍakā madhumehinām | <caesura/> karṇikāś
                        conduruviṣe viṣajuṣṭavraṇāś ca ye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.34">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.34</label>
                        <caesura/> māṃsāpāke na badhyante gudapāke ca dāruṇe | <caesura/> svabuddhyā
                        cāpi vibhajet kṛtyākṛtyāṃś ca buddhimān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.35">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.35</label>
                        <caesura/> deśaṃ doṣaṃ ca vijñāya vraṇaṃ ca vraṇakovidaḥ | <caesura/> ṛtūṃś
                        ca parisaṃkhyāya tato bandhān niveśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.36">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.36</label>
                        <caesura/> ūrdhvaṃ tiryag adhastāc ca yantraṇā trividhā smṛtā | <caesura/>
                        yathā ca badhyate bandhas tathā vakṣyāmyaśeṣataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.37</label>
                        <caesura/> ghanāṃ kavalikāṃ dattvā mṛdu caivāpi paṭṭakam | <caesura/>
                        vikeśikāmauṣadhaṃ ca nātisnigdhaṃ samācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.38">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.38</label>
                        <caesura/> prakledayatyatisnigdhā tathā rūkṣā kṣiṇoti ca | <caesura/>
                        yuktasnehā ropayati durnyastā vartma gharṣati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.39">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.39</label>
                        <caesura/> viṣamaṃ ca vraṇaṃ kuryāt stambhayet srāvayet tathā | <caesura/>
                        yathāvraṇaṃ viditvā tu yogaṃ vaidyaḥ prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.40">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.40</label>
                        <caesura/> pittaje raktaje vā'pi sakṛteva parikṣipet | <caesura/> asakṛt
                        kaphaje vā'pi vātaje ca vicakṣaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.41">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.41</label>
                        <caesura/> talena pratipīḍyātha srāvayed anulomataḥ | <caesura/> sarvāṃś ca
                        bandhān gūḍhāntān sandhīṃś ca viniveśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.42">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.42</label>
                        <caesura/> oṣṭhasyāpyeṣa sandhāne yathoddiṣṭo vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ | <caesura/>
                        buddhyotprekṣyābhiyuktena tathā cāsthiṣu jānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.43">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.43</label>
                        <caesura/> uttiṣṭhato niṣaṇṇasya śayanaṃ vā'dhigacchataḥ | <caesura/>
                        gacchato vividhair yānair nāsya duṣyati sa vraṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.44">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.44</label>
                        <caesura/> ye ca syur māṃsasaṃsthā vai tvaggatāś ca tathā vraṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/> sandhyasthikoṣṭhaprāptāś ca sirāsnāyugatās tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.18.45">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.18.45</label>
                        <caesura/> tathā'vagāḍhagambhīrāḥ sarvato viṣamasthitāḥ | <caesura/> naite
                        sādhayituṃ śakyā ṛte bandhādbhavanti hi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.4">

                        rogāḥ syuḥ śārīrāgantumānasāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.5">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.6">

                        prācyāṃ diśi sthitā devāstatpūjārthaṃ ca tacchiraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.7">

                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.8">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.9">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.10">

                        śvayathurvedanā rāgaḥ srāvaś caiva bhṛśaṃ bhavet ||// </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.11">

                        <caesura/> utthānasaṃveśanaparivartanacaṅkramaṇoccair

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.12">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.13">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.14">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.18">

                        <caesura/> madyapaś ca maireyāriṣṭāsavaśīdhusurāvikārān pariharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.19</label>
                        <caesura/> madyamamlaṃ tathā rūkṣaṃ tīkṣṇamuṣṇaṃ ca vīryataḥ | <caesura/>
                        āśukāri ca tat pītaṃ kṣipraṃ vyāpādayed draṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                        vātātaparajodhūmāvaśyāyātisevanātibhojanāniṣṭabhojanāśravaṇadarśanerṣyāmarṣabhayakrodhaśokadhyānarātrijāgaraṇaviṣamāśanaśayanopavāsavāgvyāyāmasthānacaṅkramaṇaśītavātaviruddhādhyaśanājīrṇamakṣikādyā
                        bādhāḥ pariharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.21">

                        <caesura/> vraṇinaḥ saṃprataptasya kāraṇair evam ādibhiḥ | <caesura/>
                        kṣīṇaśoṇitamāṃsasya bhuktaṃ samyaṅga jīryati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.22">

                        <caesura/> ajīrṇāt pavanādīnāṃ vibhramo balavān bhavet | <caesura/> tataḥ
                        śopharujāsrāvadāhapākānavāpnuyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.23</label>
                        <caesura/> sadā nīcanakharomṇā śucinā śuklavāsasā
                        śāntimaṅgaladevatābrāhmaṇagurupareṇa bhavitavyam iti | tat kasya hetoḥ
                        hiṃsāvihārāṇi hi mahāvīryāṇi rakṣāṃsi paśupatikuberakumārānucarāṇi
                        māṃsaśoṇitapriyatvāt kṣatajanimittaṃ vraṇinam upasarpanti satkārārthaṃ
                        jighāṃsūni vā kadācit || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.24</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra <caesura/> teṣāṃ satkārakāmānāṃ prayatetāntarātmanā
                        | <caesura/> dhūpabalyupahārāṃś ca bhakṣyāṃś caivopahārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.25</label>
                        <caesura/> te tu saṃtarpitā ātmavantamk na hiṃsyuḥ | tasmāt satatamatandrito
                        janaparivṛto nityaṃ dīpodakaśastrasragdāmapuṣpalājādyalaṅkṛte veśmani
                        sāṃpanmaṅgalamano 'nukūlāḥ kathāḥ śṛṇvannāsīta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.26">

                        <caesura/> saṃpadādyanukūlābhiḥ kathābhiḥ prītamānasaḥ | <caesura/> āśāvān
                        vyādhimokṣāya kṣipraṃ sukhamavāpnuyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.27</label>
                        <caesura/> ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvavedābhihitair aparaiś cāśīrvidhānair upādhyāyā
                        bhiṣajaś ca sandhyayo rakṣāṃ kuryuḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.28</label>
                        <caesura/> sarṣapāriṣṭapatrābhyāṃ sarpiṣā lavaṇena ca | <caesura/> dvirahnaḥ
                        kārayed dhūpaṃ daśarātramatandritaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.29</label>
                        <caesura/> chatrāmaticchatrāṃ lāṅgū(ā.ṅga)līṃ jaṭilāṃ brahmacāriṇīṃ lakṣmīṃ
                        guhāmatiguhāṃ vacāmativiṣāṃ śatavīryāṃ sahasravīryāṃ siddhārthakāṃś ca
                        śirasā dhārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.30</label>
                        <caesura/> vyajyeta bālavyajanair vraṇaṃ na ca vighaṭṭayet | <caesura/> na
                        tuden na ca kaṇḍūyec chayānaḥ paripālayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.31</label>
                        <caesura/> anena vidhinā yuktam ādāv eva niśācarāḥ | <caesura/> vanaṃ
                        keśāriṇā+ākrāntaṃ varjayanti mṛgā iva || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.32</label>
                        <caesura/> jīrṇaśālyodanaṃ snigdhamalpamuṣṇaṃ dravottaram | <caesura/>
                        bhuñjāno jāṅgalair māṃsaiḥ śīghraṃ vraṇam apohati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.33">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.33</label>
                        <caesura/> taṇḍulīyakajīvantīsuniṣaṇṇakavāstukaiḥ | <caesura/>
                        bālamūlakavātārkapaṭolaiḥ kāravellakaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.34">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.34</label>
                        <caesura/> sadāḍimaiḥ sāmalakair ghṛtabhṛṣṭaiḥ sasaindhavaiḥ | <caesura/>
                        anyair evaṃguṇair vā'pi mudgādīnāṃ rasena vā || <caesura/> śaktūn vilepīṃ
                        kulmāṣaṃ jalaṃ cāpi śṛtaṃ pibet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.35">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.35</label>
                        <caesura/> divā na nidrāvaśago nivātagṛhagocaraḥ || <caesura/> vraṇī
                        vaidyavaśe tiṣṭhan śīghraṃ vraṇamapohati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.36">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.36</label>
                        <caesura/> vraṇe śvayathurāyāsāt sa ca rāgaś ca jāgarāt | <caesura/> tau ca
                        ruk ca divāsvāpāt tāś ca mṛtyuś ca maithunāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.19.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.19.37</label>
                        <caesura/> evaṃvṛttasamācāro vraṇī saṃpadyate sukhī | <caesura/> āyuś ca
                        dīrgham āpnoti dhanvantarivaco yathā || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti śrīsuśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne vraṇitopāsanīyo
                        namaikonaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>

                <div n="20" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> viṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāto hitāhitīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.3</label>
                        <caesura/> yad vāyoḥ pathyaṃ tat pittasyāpathyam ity anena hetunā na kiṃcid
                        dravyam ekāntena hitam ahitaṃ vāstīti kecid ācāryā bruvate | tat tu na
                        samyak | iha khalu yasmād dravyāṇi svabhāvataḥ saṃyogataś caikāntahitāny
                        ekāntāhitāni hitāhitāni ca bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.4</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra ekāntahitāni jātisātmyāt salilaghṛtadugdhaudanaprabhṛtīni
                        ekāntāhitāni tu dahanapacanamāraṇādiṣu pravṛttāny agnikṣāraviṣādīni saṃyogād
                        aparāṇi viṣatulyāni bhavanti hitāhitāni tu yad vāyoḥ pathyaṃ tat
                        pittasyāpathyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.5</label>
                        <caesura/> ataḥ sarvaprāṇinām ayam āhārārthaṃ varga upadiśyate tad yathā
                        raktaśaliṣaṣṭikakaṅgukamukundakapāṇḍukapītakapramodakakālakāsanapuṣpakakardamakaśakunāhṛtasugandhakakalamanīvārakodravoddālakaśyāmākagodhūmaveṇuyavādaya
                        eṇahariṇakuraṅgamṛgamātṛkāśvadaṃṣṭrākarālakrakarakapotalāvatittirikapiñjalavartīravartikādīnāṃ
                        māṃsāni mudgavanamudgamakuṣṭhakalāyamasūramaṅgalyacaṇakahareṇvāḍhakīsatīnāḥ
                        cillivāstukasuniṣaṇṇakajīvantītaṇḍulīyakamaṇḍūkaparṇyaḥ gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ
                        saindhavadāḍimāmalakam ity eṣa vargaḥ sarvaprāṇināṃ sāmānyataḥ pathyatamaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.6</label>
                        <caesura/> tathā brahmacaryanivātaśayanoṣṇodakasnānaniśāsvapnavyāyāmāś
                        caikāntataḥ pathyatamāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.7</label>
                        <caesura/> ekāntahitāny ekāntāhitāni ca prāg upadiṣṭāni hitāhitāni tu yad
                        vāyoḥ pathyaṃ tat pittasyāpathyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.8</label>
                        <caesura/> saṃyogatas tv aparāṇi viṣatulyāni bhavanti | tad yathā
                        vallīphalakavakakarīrāmlaphalalavaṇakulatthapiṇyākadadhitailavirohipiṣṭaśuṣkaśākājāvikamāṃsamadyajāmbavacilicimamatsyagodhāvarāhāṃś
                        ca naikadhyam aśnīyāt payasā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.9</label>
                        <caesura/> rogaṃ sātmyaṃ ca deśaṃ ca kālaṃ dehaṃ ca buddhimān | <caesura/>
                        avekṣyāgnyādikān bhāvān rogavṛtteḥ prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.10ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.10ab</label>
                        <caesura/> avasthāntarabāhulyād rogādīnāṃ vyavasthitam | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.10cd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.10cd</label>
                        <caesura/> dravyaṃ necchanti bhiṣaja icchanti svastharakṣaṇe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.11</label>
                        <caesura/> dvayor anyatarādāne vadanti viṣadugdhayoḥ | <caesura/>
                        dugdhasyaikāntahitatāṃ viṣam ekāntato 'hitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.12</label>
                        <caesura/> evaṃ yuktaraseṣv eṣu dravyeṣu salilādiṣu | <caesura/>
                        ekāntahitatāṃ viddhi vatsa suśrta nānyathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.13</label>
                        <caesura/> ato 'nyāny api saṃyogādahitāni vakṣyāmaḥ na vavirūḍhadhānyair
                        vasāmadhupayoguḍamāṣair vā grāmyānūpaudakapiśitādīni nābhyavaharet na
                        payomadhubhyāṃ rohiṇīśākaṃ jātukaśākaṃ vā'śnīyāt balākāṃ vāruṇīkulmāṣābhyāṃ
                        kākamācīṃ pippalīmaricābhyāṃ nāḍībhaṅgaśākakukkuṭadadhīni ca naikadhyaṃ
                        madhu coṣṇodakānupānaṃ pittena cāmamāṃsāni surākṛśarāpāyasāṃś ca naikadhyaṃ
                        sauvīrakeṇa saha tilaśaṣkulīṃ matsyaiḥ sahekṣuvikārān guḍena kākamācīṃ
                        madhunā mūlakaṃ guḍena vārāhaṃ madhunā ca saha viruddhaṃ kṣīreṇa
                        mūlakamāmrajāmbavaśvāvicchūkaragodhāś ca sarvāṃś ca matsyān payasā viśeṣeṇa
                        cilicimaṃ kadalīphalaṃ tālaphalena payasā dadhnā takreṇa vā lakucaphalaṃ
                        payasā dadhnā māṣasūpena vā prāk payasaḥ payaso 'nte vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.14</label>
                        <caesura/> ataḥ karmaviruddhān vakṣyāmaḥ kapotān sarṣapatailabhṛṣṭānnādyāt
                        kapiñjalamayūralāvatittirigodhāś cairaṇḍadārvyagnisiddhā eraṇḍatailasiddhā
                        vā nādyāt kāṃsyabhājane daśarātraparyuṣitaṃ sarpiḥ madhu coṣṇair uṣṇe vā
                        matsyaparipacane śrṇgaveraparipacane vā siddhāṃ kākamācīṃ
                        tilakalkasiddhamupodikāśākaṃ nārikelena varāhavasā paribhṛṣṭāṃ balākāṃ
                        bhāsamaṅgāraśūlyaṃ nāśnīyād iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.15</label>
                        <caesura/> ato mānaviruddhān vakṣyāmaḥ madhvambunī madhusarpiṣī mānatastulye
                        nāśnīyāt snehau madhusnehau jalasnehau vā viśeṣādāntarīkṣodakānupānau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.16</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ rasadvandvāni rasato vīryato vipākataś ca viruddhāni
                        vakṣyāmaḥ tatra madhurāmlau rasavīryaviruddhau madhuralavaṇau ca
                        madhurakaṭukau ca sarvataḥ madhuratiktau rasavipākābhyāṃ madhurakaṣāyau ca
                        amlalavaṇau rasataḥ amlakaṭukau rasavipākābhyāṃ amlatiktāvamlakaṣāyau ca
                        sarvataḥ lavaṇakaṭukau rasavipākābhyāṃ lavaṇatiktau lavaṇakaṣāyau ca
                        sarvataḥ kaṭutiktau rasavīryābhyāṃ kaṭukaṣāyau ca tiktakaṣāyau rasataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.17</label>
                        <caesura/> taratamayogayuktāṃś ca bhāvān atirūkṣān atisnigdhān atyuṣṇān
                        atiśītān ity evam ādīn vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.18</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra | <caesura/> viruddhāny evam ādīni vīryato yāni
                        kāni ca | <caesura/> tāny ekāntāhitāny eva śeṣaṃ vidyād dhitāhitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.19</label>
                        <caesura/> vyādhim indriyadaurbalyaṃ maraṇaṃ cādhigacchati | <caesura/>
                        viruddharasavīryāṇi bhuñjāno 'nātmavān naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.20</label>
                        <caesura/> yat kiṃcid doṣam utkleśya bhuktaṃ kāyān na nirharet | <caesura/>
                        rasādiṣv ayathārthaṃ vā tad vikārāya kalpate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.21</label>
                        <caesura/> viruddhāśanajān rogān pratihanti virecanam | <caesura/> vamanaṃ
                        śamanaṃ vā'pi pūrvaṃ vā hitasevanam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.22</label>
                        <caesura/> sātymyato 'lpatayā vā'pi dīptāgnes taruṇasya ca | <caesura/>
                        snigdhavyāyāmabalināṃ viruddhaṃ vitathaṃ bhavet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.23</label>
                        <caesura/> atha vātaguṇān vakṣyāmaḥ <caesura/> pūrvaḥ samadhuraḥ snigdho
                        lavaṇaś caiva mārutaḥ | <caesura/> gururvidāhajanano raktapittābhivardhanaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.24</label>
                        <caesura/> kṣatānāṃ viṣajuṣṭānāṃ vraṇinaḥ śleṣmalāś ca | <caesura/> teṣām
                        eva viśeṣeṇa sadā rogavivardhanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.25</label>
                        <caesura/> vātalānāṃ praśastaś ca śrāntānāṃ kaphaśoṣiṇām | <caesura/> teṣām
                        eva viśeṣeṇa vraṇakledavivardhanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.26">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.26</label>
                        <caesura/> madhuraś cāvidāhī ca kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ | <caesura/> dakṣiṇo
                        mārutaḥ śreṣṭhaś cakṣuṣyo balavardhanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.27</label>
                        <caesura/> raktapittapraśamano na ca vātaprakopaṇaḥ | <caesura/> viśado
                        rūkṣaparuṣaḥ kharaḥ snehabalāpahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.28</label>
                        <caesura/> paścimo mārutastīkṣṇaḥ kaphamedoviśoṣaṇaḥ | <caesura/> sadyaḥ
                        prāṇakṣayakaraḥ śoṣaṇas tu śarīriṇām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.29</label>
                        <caesura/> uttaro mārutaḥ snigdho mṛdurmadhura eva ca | <caesura/>
                        kaṣāyānurasaḥ śīto doṣāṇāṃ cāprakopaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.20.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.20.30</label>
                        <caesura/> tasmāc ca prakṛtisthānāṃ kledano balavardhanaḥ | <caesura/>
                        kṣīṇakṣayaviṣārtānāṃ viśeṣeṇa tu pūjitaḥ || </l>

                        'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
