                <div n="21" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> ekaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāto vraṇapraśnam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.3</label>
                        <caesura/> vātapittaśleṣmāṇa eva dehasaṃbhavahetavaḥ | tair evāvyāpannair
                        adhomadhyor dhvasanniviṣṭaiḥ śarīramidaṃ dhāryate 'gāram iva sthūṇābhis
                        tisṛbhir ataś ca tristhūṇamāhureke | ta eva ca vyāpannāḥ pralayahetavaḥ |
                        tadebhir eva śoṇitacaturthaiḥ saṃbhavasth itipralayeṣv apyavirahitaṃ śarīraṃ
                        bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.4</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> narte dehaḥ kaphād asti na pittānna ca
                        mārutāt | <caesura/> śoṇitād api vā nityaṃ deha etais tu dhāryate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.5</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra vā gatigandhanayor iti dhātuḥ tapa santāpe śliṣa āliṅgane
                        eteṣāṃ kṛdvihitaiḥ pratyayair vātaḥ pittaṃ śleṣmeti ca rūpāṇi bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.6</label>
                        <caesura/> doṣasthānānyata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ tatra samāsena vātaḥ
                        śroṇigudasaṃśrayaḥ tad upary adho nābheḥ pakvāśayaḥ pakvāmāśayamadhyaṃ
                        pittasya āmāśayaḥ śleṣmaṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.7</label>
                        <caesura/> ataḥ paraṃ pañcadhā vibhajyante | tatra vātasya vātavyādhau
                        vakṣyāmaḥ pittasya yakṛtplīhānau hṛdayaṃ dṛṣtistvak pūrvoktaṃ ca
                        śleṣmaṇastūraḥśiraḥkaṇṭhasandhaya iti pūrvoktaṃ ca etāni khalu doṣāṇāṃ
                        sthānānyavyāpannānām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.8</label>
                        <caesura/> visargādānavikṣepaiḥ somasūryānilā yathā | <caesura/> dhārayanti
                        jagaddehaṃ kaphapittānilās tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.9</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra jijñāsyaṃ kiṃ pittavyatirekādanyo 'gniḥ āhosvit
                        pittamevāgnir iti | atrocyate na khalu pittavyatirekādanyo 'gnir upalabhyate
                        āgneyatvāt pitte dahanapacanādiṣvabhipravartamāneṣv agnivad upacāraḥ kriyate
                        'ntaragnir iti kṣiṇe hy agniguṇe tatsamānadravyopayogādativṛddhe
                        śītakriyopayogādāgamāc ca paśyāmo na khalu pittavyatirekādanyo 'gnir iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.10</label>
                        <caesura/> taccādṛṣṭahetukena viśeṣeṇa pakvāmāśayamadhyasthaṃ pittaṃ
                        caturvidhamannapānaṃ pacati vivecayati ca doṣarasamūtrapurīṣāṇi tatrastham
                        eva cātmaśaktyā śeṣāṇāṃ pittasthānānāṃ śarīrasya cāgnikarmaṇā'nugrahaṃ
                        karoti tasmin pitte pācako 'gnir iti saṃjñā yat tu yakṛtplīhnoḥ pittaṃ
                        tasmin rañjako 'gnir iti saṃjñā sa rasasya rāgakṛduktaḥ yat pittaṃ
                        hṛdayasaṃsthaṃ tasmin sādhako 'gnir iti saṃjñā so
                        'bhiprārthitamanorathasādhanakṛduktaḥ yaddṛṣṭyāṃ pittaṃ tasminnālocako 'gnir
                        iti saṃjñā sa rūpagrahaṇādhikṛtaḥ yat tu tvaci pittaṃ tasmin bhrājako 'gnir
                        iti saṃjñā so 'bhyaṅgapariṣekāvagāhāvalepanādīnāṃ kriyādravyāṇāṃ paktā
                        chāyānāṃ ca prakāśakaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.11</label>
                        <caesura/> pittaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ dravam pūti nīlaṃ pītaṃ tathaiva ca | <caesura/>
                        uṣṇaṃ kaṭurasaṃ caiva vidagdhaṃ cāmlam eva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.12</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ śleṣmasthānānyanuvyākhyāsyāmaḥ | tatra āmāśayaḥ
                        pittāśayasyopariṣṭhāttatpratyanīkatvād ūrdhvagatitvāt tejasaś candra iva
                        ādityasya sa caturvidhasyāhārasyādhāraḥ sa ca tatraudakair guṇair āhāraḥ
                        praklinno bhinnasaṃghātaḥ sukhajaraś ca bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.13</label>
                        <caesura/> mādhuryāt picchilatvāc ca prakleditvāt tathaiva ca | <caesura/>
                        āmāśaye saṃbhavati śleṣmā madhuraśītalaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.14</label>
                        <caesura/> sa tatrastha eva svaśaktyā śeṣāṇāṃ śleṣmasthānānāṃ śarīrasya
                        codakakarmaṇā'nugrahaṃ karoti
                        uraḥsthastrikasandhāraṇamātmavīryeṇānnarasasahitena hṛdayāvalambanaṃ karoti
                        jihvāmūlakaṇṭhastho jihvendriyasya saumyatvāt samyagrasajñāne vartate
                        śiḥrasthaḥ snehasaṃtarpaṇādhikṛtatvād indriyāṇāmātmavīryeṇānugrahaṃ karoti
                        sandhisthas tu śleṣmā sarvasandhisaṃśleṣāt sarvasandhyagranuhaṃ karoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.15</label>
                        <caesura/> śleṣmā śveto guruḥ snigdhaḥ picchilaḥ śīta eva ca | <caesura/>
                        madhurastvavigdhaḥ syādvidagdho lavaṇaḥ srṃtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.16</label>
                        <caesura/> śoṇitasya sthānaṃ yakṛtplīhānau tac ca prāgabhihitaṃ tatrastham
                        eva śeṣāṇāṃ śoṇitasthānānāmanugrahaṃ karoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.17</label>
                        <caesura/> anuṣṇaśītaṃ madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ raktaṃ ca varṇataḥ | <caesura/>
                        śoṇitaṃ guru visraṃ syādvidāhaś cāsya pittavat || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.18</label>
                        <caesura/> etāni khalu doṣasthānāni eṣu saṃcīyante doṣāḥ | prāk saṃcayahetur
                        uktaḥ | tatra saṃcitānāṃ khalu doṣāṇāṃ stabdhapūrṇakoṣṭhatā pītāvabhāsatā
                        mandoṣmatā cāṅgānāṃ gauravamālasyaṃ cayakāraṇavidveṣaś ceti liṅgāni bhavanti
                        | tatra prathamaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.19</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ prakopaṇāni vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra
                        balavadvigrahātivyāyāmavyavāyādhyayanaprapatanapradhāvanaprapīḍanābhighātalaṅghanaplavanataraṇarātrijāgaraṇabhāraharaṇagajaturagarathapadāticaryākaṭukaṣāyatiktarūkṣalaghuśītavīryaśuṣkaśākavallūravarakoddālakakoradūṣaśyāmākanīvāramudgamasūrāḍhakīhareṇukalāyaniṣpāvānaśanaviṣamāśanādhyaśanavātamūtrapurīṣaśukracchardikṣavathūdgārabāṣpavegavighātādibhir
                        viśeṣair vāyuḥ prakopamāpadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.20</label>
                        <caesura/> sa śītābhrapravāteṣu gharmānte ca viśeṣataḥ | <caesura/>
                        pratyūṣasyaparāhṇe tu jīrṇe 'nne ca prakupyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                        krodhaśokabhayāyāsopavāsavidagdhamaithunopagamanakaṭvamlalavaṇatīkṣṇoṣṇalaghuvidāhitilatailapiṇyākakulatthasarṣapātasīharitakaśākagodhāmatsyājāvikamāṃsadadhitakrakūrcikāmastusauvīrakasurāvikārāmlaphalakaṭvaraprabhṛtibhiḥ
                        pittaṃ prakopamāpadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.22</label>
                        <caesura/> taduṣṇair uṣṇakāle ca meghānte ca viṣeśataḥ | <caesura/>
                        madhyāhne cārdharātre ca jīryatyanne ca kupyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                        divāsvapnāvyāyāmālasyamadhurāmlalavaṇaśītasnigdhagurupicchilābhiṣyandihāyanakayavakanaiṣadhetkaṭamāṣamahāmāṣagodhūma-tila-piṣṭa-vikṛtidadhidugdhakṛśarāpāyasekṣu-vikārānūpaudakamāṃsavasābisamṛṇālakaserukaśṛṅgāṭakamadhura-vallī-phalasamaśanādhyaśanaprabhṛtibhiḥ
                        śleṣmā prakopamāpadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.24</label>
                        <caesura/> sa śītaiḥ śītakāle ca vasante ca viśeṣataḥ | <caesura/> pūrvāhṇe
                        ca pradoṣe ca bhuktamātre prakupyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.25</label>
                        <caesura/> pittaprakopaṇair eva cābhīkṣṇaṃ dravasnigdhagurubhir āhārair
                        divāsvapnakrodhānalātapaśramābhighātājīrṇaviruddhādhyaśanādibhir viśeṣair
                        asṛk prakopamāpadyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.26">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.26</label>
                        <caesura/> yasmādraktmaṃ vinā doṣair nā kadācit prakupyati | <caesura/>
                        tasmāt tasya yathādoṣaṃ kālaṃ vidyātprakopaṇe || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.27</label>
                        <caesura/> teṣāṃ prakopāt
                        koṣṭhatodasaṃcaraṇāmlikāpipāsāparidāhānnadveṣahṛdayotkledāś ca jāyante |
                        tatra dvitīyaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.28</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ prasaraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ teṣām ebhir ātaṅkaviśeṣaiḥ
                        prakupitānāṃ (paryuṣita) kiṇvodakapiṣṭasamavāya ivodriktānāṃ prasaro bhavati
                        | teṣāṃ vāyur gatimattvāt prasaraṇahetuḥ saty apy acaitanye | sa hi
                        rajobhūyiṣṭhaḥ rajaś ca pravartakaṃ sarvabhāvānām | yathā mahānudakasaṃcayo
                        'tivṛddhaḥ setumavadāryāpareṇodakena vyāmiśraḥ sarvataḥ pradhāvati evaṃ
                        doṣāḥ kadācidekaśo dviśaḥ samastāḥ śoṇitasahitā vā'nekadhā prasaranti | tad
                        yathā vātaḥ pittaṃ śleṣmā śoṇitaṃ vātapitte vātaśleṣmāṇau pittaśleṣmāṇau
                        vātaśoṇite pittaśoṇite śleṣmaśoṇite vātapittaśoṇitāni vātaśleṣmaśoṇitāni
                        pittaśleṣmaśoṇitāni vātapittakaphāḥ vātapittakaphaśoṇitāni ity evaṃ
                        pañcadaśadhā prasanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.29</label>
                        <caesura/> kṛtsne 'rdhe 'vayave vā'pi yatrāṅge kupito bhṛśam | <caesura/>
                        doṣo vikāraṃ nabhasi meghavattatra varṣati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.30</label>
                        <caesura/> nātyarthaṃ kupitaś cāpi līno mārgeṣu tiṣṭhati | <caesura/>
                        niṣpratyanīkaḥ kālena hetumāsādya kupyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.31</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra vāyoḥ pittasthānagatasya pittavat pratīkāraḥ pittasya ca
                        kaphasthānagatasya kaphavat kaphasya ca vātasthānagatasya vātavat eṣa
                        kriyāvibhāgaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.32</label>
                        <caesura/> evaṃ prakupitānāṃ prasaratāṃ ca vāyor vimārgagamanāṭopau
                        oṣacoṣaparidāhadhūmāyanāni pittasya arocakāvipākāṅgasādāś chardiś ceti
                        śleṣmaṇo liṅgāni bavanti tatra tṛtīyaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.33">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.33</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ sthānasaṃśrayaṃ | evaṃ prakupitāḥ tāṃstān
                        śarīrapradeśānāgamya tāṃstān vyādhīn janayanti | te yadodarasanniveśaṃ
                        kurvanti tadā gulmavidradhyudarāgnisaṅgānāhavisūcikātisāraprabhṛtīn
                        janayanti bastigatāḥ pramehāśmarīmūtrāghātamūtradoṣaprabhṛtīn vṛṣaṇagatā
                        vṛddhīḥ meḍhragatā niruddhaprakaśopadaṃśaśūkadoṣaprabhṛtīn gudagatā
                        bhagandarārśaḥprabhṛtīn ūrdhvajatrugatāstūrdhvajān tavaṅnāṃsaśoṇitasthāḥ
                        kṣudrarogān kuṣṭhāni visarpāṃś ca medogatā
                        granthyapacyarbudagalagaṇḍālajīprabhṛtīn asthigatā vidradhyanuśayīprabhṛtīn
                        pādagatāḥ ślīpadavātaśoṇitavātakaṇṭakaprabhṛtīn sarvāṅgāgatā
                        jvarasaravāṅgarogaprabhṛtīn teṣāmevamabhiniviṣṭānāṃ pūrvarūpaprādurbhāvaḥ
                        taṃ pratirogaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | tatra pūrvarūpagateṣu caturthaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.34">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.34</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ vyādherdarśanaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
                        śophārbudagranthividradhivisarpaprabhṛtīnāṃ pravyaktalakṣaṇatā
                        jvarātīsāraprabhṛtīnāṃ ca | tatra pañcamaḥ kriyākālaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.35">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.35</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvameteṣāmavadīrṇānāṃ braṇabhāvamāpannānāṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ
                        kriyākālaḥ jvarātisāraprabhṛtīnāṃ ca dīrghakālānubandhaḥ |
                        tatrāpratikriyamāṇe 'sādhyatām upayānti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.36">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.36</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra | <caesura/> saṃcayaṃ ca prakopaṃ ca prasaraṃ
                        sthānasaṃśrayam | <caesura/> vyaktiṃ bhedaṃ ca yo vetti doṣāṇāṃ sa
                        bhavedbhiṣak || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.37">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.37</label>
                        <caesura/> saṃcaye 'pahṛtā doṣā labhante nottarā gatīḥ | <caesura/> te
                        tūttarāsu gatiṣu bhavanti balavattarāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.38">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.38</label>
                        <caesura/> sarvair bhāvais tribhir vā'pi dvābhyāmekena vā punaḥ | <caesura/>
                        saṃsarge kupitaḥ kruddhaṃ doṣaṃ doṣo 'nudhāvati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.39">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.39</label>
                        <caesura/> saṃsarge yo garīyān syād upakramyaḥ sa vai bhavet | <caesura/>
                        śeṣadoṣāvirodhena sannipāte tathaiva ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.21.40">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.21.40</label>
                        <caesura/> vṛṇoti yasmāt rūḍhe 'pi vraṇavas tu na naśyati | <caesura/>
                        ādehadhāraṇāttasmād draṇa ity ucyate budhaiḥ || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrashtāne vraṇapraśnādhyāyo
                        nāmaikaviṃśodhyāyaḥ </p>
                </div>



                <div n="22" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāto vraṇāsrāvavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyamaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.3</label>
                        <caesura/> tvaṅnāṃsasirāsnāyvasthisandhikoṣṭhamarmāṇītyaṣṭau vraṇavastūni |
                        atra sarvavraṇasanniveśaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.4</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra ādyaikavastusanniveśī tvagbhedī vraṇaḥ sūpacaraḥ śeṣāḥ
                        svayamavaddīryamāṇā durupacārāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.5</label>
                        <caesura/> tatrāyataś caturasro vṛttastripuṭaka iti vraṇākṛtisamāsaḥ śeṣās
                        tu vikṛtākṛtayo durupakramā bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.6</label>
                        <caesura/> sarva eva vraṇāḥ kṣipraṃ saṃrohantyātmavatāṃ subhiṣagbhiś
                        copakrāntāḥ anātmavatāmajñaiś copakrāntāḥ praduṣyanti pravṛddhatvāc ca
                        doṣāṇāṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.7</label>
                        <caesura/> tatrātisaṃvṛto 'tivivṛto 'tikaṭhino 'timṛdurutsanno 'vasanno
                        'tiśīto 'tyuṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇaraktapītaśuklādīnāṃ varṇānām anyatamavarṇo bhairavaḥ
                        pūtipūyamāṃsasirāsnāyuprabhṛtibhiḥ pūrṇaḥ
                        pūtipūyāsrāvyunmārgyutsaṅgyamanojñadarśanagandho 'tyarthaṃ vedanāvān
                        dāhapākarāgakaṇḍūśophapiḍakopadruto 'tyarthaṃ duṣṭaśoṇitāsrāvī
                        dīrghakālānubandhī ceti duṣṭavraṇaliṅgāni | tasya doṣocchrāyeṇa ṣaṭtvaṃ
                        vibhajya yathāsvaṃ pratīkāre prayateta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.8a">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.8a</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ sarvasrāvān vakṣyāmaḥ tatra ghṛṣṭāsu chinnāsu vā
                        tvakṣu sphoṭeṣu bhinneṣu vidāriteṣu vā salilaprakāśo bhavatyāsrāvaḥ
                        kiṃcidvisraḥ pītāvabhāsaś ca māṃsagataḥ sadyaś chinnāsu sirāsu
                        raktātipravṛttiḥ pakvāsu ca toyanāḍībhir iva toyāgamanaṃ pūyasya āsrāvaś
                        cātra tanur vicchinnaḥ picchilo 'valambī śyāvo 'vaśyāyapratimaś ca
                        snāyugataḥ snigdho ghanaḥ siṃghāṇakapratimaḥ saraktaś ca asthigato
                        'sthanyabhihate sphuṭite bhinne doṣāvadārite vā doṣabhakṣitatvād asthi
                        niḥsāraṃ śuktidhautamivābhāti āsrāvaś cātra majjamiśraḥ sarudhiraḥ snigdhaś
                        ca saṃdhigataḥ pīḍyamāno na pravartate
                        ākuñcanaprasāraṇonnamanavinamanapradhāvanotkāsanapravāhaṇaiś ca sravati
                        āsrāvaś cātra picchilo 'valambī saphenapūyarudhironmathitaś ca koṣṭhagato
                        'sṛṅnūtrapurīṣapūyodakāni sravati marmagatas tvagādiṣv avaruddhatvān nocyate
                        | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.8b">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.8b</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra tvagādigatānāmāsrāvāṇāṃ yathākramaṃ
                        pāruṣyaśyāvāvaśyāyadadhimastukṣārodakamāṃsadhāvanapulākodakasannibhatvāni
                        mārutādbhavanti pittād
                        gomedagomūtrabhasmaśaṅkhakaṣāyodakamādhvīkatailasannibhatvāni
                        pittavadraktādativisratvaṃ ca
                        kaphānnavanītakāsīsamajjapiṣṭatilanārikelodakavarāhavasāsannibhatvāni
                        sannipātānnārikelodakair
                        vārukarasakāñjikaprasādārukodakapriyaṅguphalayakṛnmudgayūṣasavarṇatvānīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.9</label>
                        <caesura/> ślokau cātra bhavataḥ | <caesura/> pakvāśayādasādhyas tu
                        pulākodakasannibhiḥ | <caesura/> kṣārodakanibhaḥ srāvo varjyo
                        raktāśayātsravan || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.10</label>
                        <caesura/> āmāśayāt kalāyāmbhonibhaś ca trikasandhijaḥ | <caesura/>
                        srāvānetān parīkṣyādau tataḥ karmācared bhiṣak ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.11</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ sarvavraṇavedanā vakṣyāmaḥ
                        todanabhedanatāḍanacchedanāyamanamanthanavikṣepaṇacum
                        cumāyananirdahanāvabhañjanasphoṭanavidāraṇotpāṭanakampanavividhaśūlaviśleṣaṇavikiraṇapūraṇastambhanasvapnākuñcanāṅkuśikāḥ
                        saṃbhavanti animittavividhavedanāprādurbhāvo vā muhurmuhur yatrāgacchanti
                        vedanāviśeṣāstaṃ vātikam iti vidyāt oṣacoṣaparidāhadhūmāyanāni yatra
                        gātramaṅgārāvakīrṇam iva pacyate yatra coṣmābhivṛddhiḥ kṣate kṣārāvasiktavac
                        ca vedanāviśeṣāstaṃ paittikam iti vidyāt pittavadraktasamutthaṃ jānīyāt
                        kaṇḍūrgurutvaṃ suptatvam upadeho 'lpavedanatvaṃ stambhaḥ śaityaṃ ca yatra
                        taṃ ślaiṣmikam iti vidyāt yatra sarvāsāṃ vedanānām utpattis taṃ sānnipātikam
                        iti vidyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.12</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvaṃ vraṇavarṇān vakṣyāmaḥ bhasmakapotāsthivarṇaḥ paruṣo
                        'ruṇaḥ kṛṣṇa iti mārutajasya nīlaḥ pīto haritaḥ śyāvaḥ kṛṣṇo raktaḥ kapilaḥ
                        piṅgala iti raktapittasamutthayoḥ śvetaḥ snigdhaḥ pāṇḍur iti śleṣmajasya
                        sarvavarṇopetaḥ sānnipātika iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.22.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.22.13</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> na kevalaṃ vraṇeṣūkto
                        vedanāvarṇasaṃgrahaḥ | <caesura/> sarvaśophavikāreṣu vraṇaval lakṣayed
                        bhiṣak || </l>
                </div>




                <div n="23" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>trayoviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaḥ kṛtyākṛtyavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.3</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra vayaḥsthānāṃ dṛḍhānāṃ prāṇavatāṃ sattvavatāṃ ca sucikitsyā
                        vraṇāḥekasmin vā puruṣe yatraitad guṇacatuṣṭayaṃ tasya sukhasādhanīyatamāḥ |
                        tatra vayaḥsthānāṃ pratyagradhātutvād āśu vraṇā rohanti dṛḍhānāṃ
                        sthirabahumāṃsatvāc chastram avacāryamāṇaṃ sirāsnāyvādiviśeṣān na prāpnoti
                        prāṇavatāṃ vedanābhighātāhārayantraṇādibhir na glānir utpadyate sattvavatāṃ
                        dāruṇair api kriyāviśeṣair na vyathā bhavati tasmād eteṣāṃ
                        sukhasādhanīyatamāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.4</label>
                        <caesura/> ta eva viparītaguṇā vṛddhakṛśālpaprāṇabhīruṣu draṣṭavyāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                        sphikpāyuprajananalalāṭagaṇḍauṣṭhapṛṣṭhakarṇaphalakoṣodarajatrumukhābhyantarasaṃsthāḥ
                        sukharopaṇīyā vraṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                        akṣidantanāsāpāṅgaśrotranābhijaṭharasevanīnitambapārśvakukṣivakṣaḥkakṣāstanasandhibhāgagatāḥ
                        saphenapūyaraktānilavāhino 'ntaḥśalyāś ca duścikitsyāḥ adhobhāgāś
                        cordhvabhāganirvāhiṇo romāntopanakhamarmajaṅghāsthisaṃśritāś ca bhagandaram
                        api cāntarmukhaṃ sevanīkuṭakāsthisaṃśritam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.7</label>
                        <caesura/> kuṣṭhināṃ viṣajuṣṭānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ madhumehinām | <caesura/> vraṇāḥ
                        kṛcchreṇa sidhyanti yeṣāṃ cāpi vraṇe vraṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                        avapāṭikāniruddhaprakaśasanniruddhagudajaṭharagranthikṣatakrimayaḥ
                        pratiśyāyajāḥ koṣṭhajāś ca tvagdoṣiṇāṃ pramehiṇāṃ vā ye parikṣateṣu dṛśyante
                        śarkarā sikatāmeho vātakuṇḍalikā'ṣṭhīlā dantaśarkaropakuśaḥ kaṇṭhaśālūkaṃ
                        niṣkoṣaṇadūṣitāś ca dantaveṣṭā
                        visarpāsthikṣatoraḥkṣatavraṇagranthiprabhṛtayaś ca yāpyāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.9</label>
                        <caesura/> sādhyā yāpyatvam āyānti yāpyāś cāsādhyatāṃ tathā | <caesura/>
                        ghnanti prāṇān asādhyās tu narāṇām akriyāvatām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.10</label>
                        <caesura/> yāpanīyaṃ vijānīyāt kriyā dhārayate tu yam | <caesura/> kriyāyāṃ
                        tu nivṛttāyāṃ sadya eva vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.11</label>
                        <caesura/> prāptā kriyā dhārayati yāpyavayādhitam āturam | <caesura/>
                        prapatiṣyadivāgāraṃ viṣkambhaḥ sādhuyojitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.12</label>
                        <caesura/> ata ūrdhvam asādhyān vakṣyāmaḥ māṃsapiṇḍavad udgatāḥ prasekino
                        'ntaḥpūyavedanāvanto 'śvāpānavad udvṛttauṣṭhāḥ kecit kaṭhinā gośṛṅgavad
                        unnatamṛdumāṃsaprarohāḥ apare duṣṭarudhirāsrāviṇastanuśītapicchilasrāviṇo vā
                        madhyonnatāḥ kecid avasannaśuṣiraparyantāḥ śaṇatūlavat snāyujālavanto
                        durdarśanāḥ vasāmedomajjamastuluṅgasrāviṇaś ca doṣasamutthāḥ
                        pītāsitamūtrapurīṣavātavāhinaś ca koṣṭhasthāḥ ta evobhayatobhāgavraṇamukheṣu
                        pūyaraktanirvāhiṇaḥ (ā.kṣīṇamāṃsānāṃ ca) sarvato gatayaś cāṇumukhā
                        māṃsabudbudavantaḥ saśabdavātavāhinaś ca śiraḥkaṇṭhasthāḥ kṣīṇamāṃsānāṃ ca
                        pūyaraktanirvāhiṇo 'rocakāvipākakāsaśvāsopadravayuktāḥ bhinne vā śiraḥkapāle
                        yatra mastuluṅgadarśanaṃ tridoṣaliṅgaprādurbhāvaḥ kāsaśvāsau vā yasyeti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.13</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra | <caesura/> vasāṃ medo 'tha majjānaṃ mastuluṅgaṃ
                        ca yaḥ sravet | <caesura/> āgantus tu vraṇaḥ sidhyen na sidhyed
                        doṣasaṃbhavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.14</label>
                        <caesura/> amarmopahite deśe sirāsandhyasthivarjite | <caesura/> vikāro yo
                        'nuparyeti tad asādhyasya lakṣaṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.15</label>
                        <caesura/> krameṇopacayaṃ prāpya dhatūn anugataḥ śanaiḥ | <caesura/> na
                        śakya unmūlayituṃ vṛddho vṛkṣa ivāmayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.16</label>
                        <caesura/> sa sthiratvān mahattvāc ca dhātvanukramaṇena ca | <caesura/>
                        nihantyauṣadhavīryāṇi mantrān duṣṭagraho yathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.17</label>
                        <caesura/> ato yo viparītaḥ syāt sukhasādhyaḥ sa ucyate | <caesura/>
                        abaddhamūlaḥ kṣupako yadvad utpāṭane sukhaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.18</label>
                        <caesura/> tribhir doṣair anākrāntaḥ śyāvauṣṭhaḥ piḍakī samaḥ | <caesura/>
                        avedano nirāsrāvo vraṇaḥ śuddha ihocyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.19</label>
                        <caesura/> kapotavarṇapratimā yasyāntāḥ kledavarjitāḥ | <caesura/> sthirāś
                        cipiṭikāvanto rohatīti tam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.20</label>
                        <caesura/> rūḍhavartmānam agranthim aśūnam arujaṃ vraṇam | <caesura/>
                        tvaksavarṇaṃ samatalaṃ samyag rūḍhaṃ vinirdiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.23.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.23.21</label>
                        <caesura/> doṣaprakopād vyāyāmādabhighātādajīrṇataḥ | <caesura/> harṣāt
                        krodhād bhayād vā 'pi vraṇo rūḍho 'pi dīryate || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne kṛtyākṛtyavidhirnāma
                        trayoviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                </div>

                <div n="24" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> caturviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athāto vyādhisamuddeśīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.3</label>
                        <caesura/> dvividhās tu vyādhayaḥ śastrasādhyāḥ snehādikriyāsādhyāś ca |
                        tatra śastrasādhyeṣu snehādikriyā na pratiṣidhyate snehādikriyāsādhyeṣu
                        śastrakarma na kriyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.4</label>
                        <caesura/> asmin punaḥ śāstre sarvatantrasāmānyāt sarveṣāṃ vyādhīnāṃ
                        yathāsthūlam avarodhaḥ kriyate | prāgabhihitaṃ tadduḥkhasaṃyogā vyādhaya iti
                        | tac ca duḥkhaṃ trividhaṃ ādhyātmikaṃ ādhibhautikaṃ ādhidaivikam iti | tat
                        tu saptavidhe vyādhāv upanipatati | te punaḥ saptavidhā vyādhayaḥ tad yathā
                        ādibalapravṛttāḥ janmabalapravṛttāḥ doṣabalapravṛttāḥ saṃghātabalapravṛttāḥ
                        kālabalapravṛttāḥ daivabalapravṛttāḥ svabhāvabalapravṛttā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.5</label>
                        <caesura/> tatrādibalapravṛttā ye śukraśoṇitadoṣānvayāḥ
                        kuṣṭhārśaḥprabhṛtayaḥ te 'pi dvividhāḥ mātṛjāḥ pitṛjāś ca |
                        janmabalapravṛttā ye māturapacārāt
                        paṅgujātyandhabadhiramūkaminminavāmanaprabhṛtayo jāyante te 'pi dvividhā
                        rasakṛtāḥ dauhṛdāpacārakṛtāś ca | doṣabalapravṛttā ya ātaṅkasamutpannā
                        mithyāhārācārakṛtāś ca te 'pi dvividhāḥ āmāśayasamutthāḥ pakvāśayasamutthāś
                        ca | punaś ca dvividhāḥ śārīrā mānasāś ca | ta ete ādhyātmikāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.6</label>
                        <caesura/> saṃghātabalapravṛttā ya āgantavo durbalasya balavadvigrahāt te
                        'pi dvividhāḥ śastrakṛtā vyālakṛtāś ca | ete ādhibhautikāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.7a">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.7a</label>
                        <caesura/> kālabalapravṛttā ye śītoṣṇavātavarṣāprabhṛtinimittāḥ te 'pi
                        dvividhāḥ vyāpannartukṛtā avyāpannartukṛtāś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.7</label>
                        <caesura/> daivabalapravṛttā ye devadrohādabhiśastakā atharvaṇakṛtā
                        upasargajāś ca te 'pi dvividhāḥ vidyudaśanikrtāḥ piśācādikṛtāś ca punaś ca
                        dvividhāḥ saṃsargajā ākasmikāś ca | svabhāvabalapravṛttāḥ
                        kṣutpipāsājarāmṛtyunidrāprabhṛtayaḥ te 'pi dvividhāḥ kālakṛtā akālakṛtāś ca
                        tatra parirakṣaṇakṛtāḥ kālakṛtāḥ aparirakṣaṇakṛtā akālakṛtāḥ | ete
                        ādhidaivikāḥ | atra sarvavyādhyavarodhaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.8</label>
                        <caesura/> sarveṣāṃ ca vyādhīnāṃ vātapittaśleṣmāṇa eva mūlaṃ talliṅgatvād
                        dṛṣṭaphalatvād āgamāc ca | yathā hi kṛtsnaṃ vikārajātaṃ viśvarūpeṇāvasthitaṃ
                            sattva<pc> </pc>rajas<pc> </pc>tamāṃsi na vyatiricyante evam eva kṛtsnaṃ
                        vikārajātaṃ viśvarūpeṇāvasthitam avyatiricya vātapittaśleṣmāṇo vartante |
                        doṣadhātumalasaṃsargād āyatanaviśeṣān nimittataś caiṣāṃ vikalpaḥ |
                        doṣadūṣiteṣv atyarthaṃ dhātuṣu saṃjñā kriyate rasajo 'yaṃ śoṇitajo 'yaṃ
                        māṃsajo 'yaṃ medojo 'yaṃ asthijo 'yaṃ majjajo 'yaṃ śukrajo 'yam vyādhir iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.9</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra
                        annāśraddhārocakāvipākāṅgamardajvarahṛllāsatṛptigauravahṛtpāṇḍurogamārgoparodhakārśyavairasyāṅgasādākālavalipalitadarśanaprabhṛtayo
                        rasadoṣajā vikārāḥ
                        kuṣṭhavisarpapiḍakāmaśakanīlikātilakālakanyacchavyaṅgendraluptaplīhavidradhigulmavātaśoṇitārśo
                        'rbudāṅgamardāsṛgdararaktapittaprabhṛtayo raktadoṣajāḥ gudamukhameḍhrapākāś
                        ca adhimāṃsārbudārśo
                        'dhijihvopajihvopakuśagalaśuṇḍikālajīmāṃsasaṃghātauṣṭhaprakopagalagaṇḍagaṇḍamālāprabhṛtayo
                        māṃsadoṣajāḥ
                        granthivṛddhigalagaṇḍārbudamedojauṣṭhaprakopamadhumehātisthaulyātisvedaprabhṛtayo
                        medodoṣajāḥ adhyasthyadhidantāsthitodaśūlakunakhaprabhṭayo 'sthidoṣajāḥ
                        tamodarśanamūrcchābhramaparvasthūlamūlārurjanmanetrābhisyandaprabhṛtayo
                        majjadoṣajāḥ klaibyāpraharṣaśukrāśmarīśukramehaśukradoṣādayaś ca taddoṣajāḥ
                        tvagdoṣāḥ saṅgo 'tipravṛttirayathāpravṛttir vā malāyatanadoṣāḥ indriyāṇām
                        apravṛttir ayathā pravṛttir vendriyāyatanadoṣāḥ ity eṣa samāsa uktaḥ
                        vistaraṃ nimittāni caiṣāṃ pratirogaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.10</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> kupitānāṃ hi doṣāṇāṃ śarīre
                        paridhāvatām | <caesura/> yatra saṅgaḥ khavaiguṇyād vyādhis tatropajāyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.11</label>
                        <caesura/> bhūyo 'tra jijñāsyaṃ kiṃ vātādīnāṃ jvarādīnāṃ ca nityaḥ saṃśleṣaḥ
                        paricchedo vā iti yadi nityaḥ saṃśleṣaḥ syāt tarhi nityāturāḥ sarva eva
                        prāṇinaḥ syuḥ athāpy anyathā vātādīnāṃ jvarādīnāṃ cānyatra vartamānānām
                        anyatra liṅgaṃ na bhavatīti kṛtvā yad ucyate vātādayo jvarādīnāṃ mūlānīti
                        tan na | atrocyate doṣān pratyākhyāya jvarādayo na bhavanti atha ca na
                        nityaḥ saṃbandhaḥ yathā hi vidyudvātāśanivarṣāṇyākāśaṃ pratyākhyāya na
                        bhavanti saty apy ākāśe kadācin na bhavanti atha ca nimittatas tata
                        evotpattir iti taraṅgabudbudādayaś codakaviśeṣāḥ eva vātādīnāṃ jvarādīnāṃ ca
                        nāpy evam saṃśleṣo na paricchedaḥ śāśvatikaḥ atha ca nimittata evotpattir
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.24.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.24.12</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavati cātra | <caesura/> vikāraparimāṇaṃ ca saṃkhyā caiṣāṃ
                        pṛthak pṛthak | <caesura/> vistareṇottare tantre sarvā bādhāś ca vakṣyate || </l>


                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne vyādhisamuddeśīyo nāma
                        caturviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                </div>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.4">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.5">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.6">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.7">

                        kṣudrarogāś ca puppuṭau tāludantajau || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.8</label>
                        <caesura/> tuṇḍikerī gilāyuś ca pūrvaṃ ye ca prapākiṇaḥ | <caesura/> bastis
                        tathā'śmarīhetormedojā ye ca kecana || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.9"</label>
                        <caesura/> lekhyāś catasro rohiṇyaḥ kilāsam upajihvikā | <caesura/> medojo
                        dantavaidarbho granthir vartmādhijihvikā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.10ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.10ab</label>
                        <caesura/> arśāṃsi maṇḍalaṃ māṃsakandī māṃsonnatis tathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.10cd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.10cd</label>
                        <caesura/> vedhyāḥ sirā bahuvidhā mūtravṛddhirdakodaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.11-12ab">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.11-12ab</label>
                        <caesura/> eṣyā nāḍyaḥ saśalyāś ca vraṇā unmārgiṇaś ca | <caesura/> āhāryāḥ
                        śarkarās tisro dantakarṇamalo 'śmarī || <caesura/> śalyāni mūḍhagarbhāś ca
                        varcaś ca nicitaṃ gude | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.12cd">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.12cd</label>
                        <caesura/> srāvyā vidradhayaḥ pañca bhaveyuḥ sarvajādṛte || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.13</label>
                        <caesura/> kuṣṭhāni vāyuḥ sarujaḥ śopho yaś caikadeśajaḥ | <caesura/>
                        pālyāmayāḥ ślīpadāni viṣajuṣṭaṃ ca śoṇitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.14</label>
                        <caesura/> arbudāni visarpāś ca granthayaś cāditas tu ye | <caesura/> trayas
                        trayaś copadaṃśāḥ stanarogā vidārikā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.15</label>
                        <caesura/> suṣiro galaśālūkaṃ kaṇṭakāḥ kṛmidantakaḥ | <caesura/> dantaveṣṭaḥ
                        sopakuśaḥ śītādo dantapuppuṭaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.16</label>
                        <caesura/> pittāsṛkkaphajāś cauṣṭhyāḥ kṣudrarogāś ca bhūyaśaḥ | <caesura/>
                        sīvyā medaḥsamutthāś ca bhinnāḥ sulikhitā gadāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.17</label>
                        <caesura/> sadyovraṇāś ca ye caiva calasandhivyapāśritāḥ | <caesura/> na
                        kṣārāgniviṣair juṣṭā na ca mārutavāhinaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.25.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.25.18</label>

                <div n="26" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaḥ pranaṣṭaśalyavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantiriḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.3</label>
                        <caesura/> śala śvala āśugamane dhātuḥ tasya śalyam iti rūpam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.4</label>
                        <caesura/> tad dvividhaṃ śārīram āgantukaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.5</label>
                        <caesura/> sarvaśarīrābādhakaraṃ śalyaṃ tadihopadiśyata ity ataḥ
                        śalyaśāstram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.6</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra śārīraṃ romanakhādi dhātavo 'nnamalā doṣāś ca duṣṭāḥ āgantv
                        api śārīraśalyavyatirekeṇa yāvanto bhāvā duḥkham utpādayanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.7</label>
                        <caesura/> adhikāro hi lohaveṇuvṛkṣatṛṇaśṛṅgāsthimayeṣu tatrāpi viśeṣato
                        loheṣveva viśasanārthopapannatvāllohasya lohānām api durvāratvād
                        aṇumukhatvād dūraprayojanakaratvāc ca śara evādhikṛtaḥ | sa dvividhaḥ karṇī
                        ślakṣṇaś ca prāyeṇa vividhavṛkṣapatrapuṣpaphalatulyākṛtayo vyākhyātā
                        vyālamṛgapakṣivaktrasadṛśāś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.8</label>
                        <caesura/> sarvaśalyānāṃ tu mahatāmaṇūnāṃ vā pañcavidho gativiśeṣa ūrdhvam
                        adho 'rvācīnas tiryag ṛjur iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.9-10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.9-10</label>
                        <caesura/> tāni vegakṣayāt pratighātād vā tvagādiṣu vraṇavastuṣv
                        avatiṣṭhante dhamanīsroto 'sthivivarapeśīprabhṛtiṣu vā śarīrapradeśeṣu ||
                            <label>1931 ed. 1.26.10</label> tatra śalyalakṣaṇam ucyamānam upadhāraya
                        | tat tu dvividhaṃ sāmānyaṃ vaiśeṣikaṃ ca | śyāvaṃ piḍakācitaṃ
                        śophavedanāvantaṃ muhurmuhuḥ śoṇitāsrāviṇaṃ budbudavad unnataṃ mṛdumāṃsaṃ ca
                        vraṇaṃ jānīyāt saśalyo 'yam iti | sāmānyam etal lakṣaṇam uktam | vaiśeṣikaṃ
                        tu tvaggate vivarṇaḥ śopho bhavaty āyataḥ kaṭhinaś ca māṃsagate
                        śophābhivṛddhiḥ śalyamārgān upasaṃrohaḥ pīḍanāsahiṣṇutā coṣapākau ca
                        peśyantarasthe 'py etad eva coṣaśophavarjaṃ sirāgate sirādhmānam sirāśūlaṃ
                        sirāśophaś ca snāyugate snāyujālotkṣepaṇaṃ saṃrambhaś cogrā ruk ca srotogate
                        srotasāṃ svakarmaguṇahāniḥ; dhamanīsthe saphenaṃ raktam īrayann anilaḥ
                        saśabdo nirgacchaty aṅgamardaḥ pipāsā hṛllāsaś ca asthigate
                        vividhavedanāprādurbhāvaḥ śophaś ca asthivivaragate 'sthipūrṇatā'sthitodaḥ
                        saṃharṣo balavāṃś ca sandhigate 'sthivacceṣṭoparamaś ca koṣṭhagata
                        āṭopānāhau mūtrapurīṣāhāradarśanaṃ ca vraṇamukhāt marmagate marmaviddhāvac
                        ceṣṭate | sūkṣmagatiṣu śalyeṣv etāny eva lakṣaṇāny aspaṣṭāni bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.11</label>
                        <caesura/> mahānty alpāni vā śuddhadehānām anulomasanniviṣṭāni rohanti
                        viśeṣataḥ kaṇṭhasrotaḥsirātvakpeśyasthivivareṣu
                        doṣaprakopavyāyāmābhighātājīrṇebhyaḥ pracalitāni punarbādhante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.12</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra tvakpranaṣṭe snigdhasvinnāyāṃ
                        mṛnmāṣayavagodhūmagomayamṛditāyāṃ tvaci yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati
                        tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt styānaghṛtamṛccandanakalkair vā pradigdhāyāṃ
                        śalyoṣmaṇā+āśu visarati ghṛtam upaśuṣyati vā lepo yatra tatra śalyaṃ
                        vijānīyāt māṃsapranaṣṭe snehasvedādibhiḥ kriyāviśeṣair aviruddair āturam
                        upapādayet karśitasya tu śithilībhūtam anavabaddhaṃ kṣubhyamāṇaṃ yatra
                        saṃrambhaṃ vedanāṃ vā janayati tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt
                        koṣṭhāsthisandhipeśīvivareṣv avasthitam evam eva parīkṣeta
                        sirādhamanīsrotaḥsnāyupranaṣṭe khaṇḍacakrasaṃyukte yāne vyādhitam āropyāśu
                        viṣame 'dhvani yāyād yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra śalyaṃ jānīyāt
                        asthipranaṣṭe snehasvedopapannānyasthīni bandhanapīḍanābhyāṃ bhṛśam upācared
                        yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra śalyaṃ jānīyāt sandhipranaṣṭe
                        snehasvedopapannān sandhīn prasaraṇākuñcanabandhanapīḍanair bhṛśam upācaret
                        yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra śalyaṃ vijānīyāt marmapranaṣṭe tv
                        ananyabhāvān marmaṇām uktaṃ parīkṣaṇaṃ bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.13</label>
                        <caesura/> sāmānyalakṣaṇam api ca
                        hastiskandhāśvapṛṣṭhaparvatadrumārohaṇadhanurvyāyāmadrutayānaniyuddhādhvagamanalaṅghanaprataraṇaplavanavyāyāmair
                        jṛmbhodgārakāsakṣavathuṣṭhīvanahasanaprāṇāyāmair
                        vātamūtrapurīṣaśukrotsargair vā yatra saṃrambho vedanā vā bhavati tatra
                        śalyaṃ jānīyāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.14</label>
                        <caesura/> bhavanti cātra | <caesura/> yasmiṃs todādayo deśo suptatā
                        gurutā'pi ca | <caesura/> ghaṭṭate bahuśo yatra srūyate tudyate 'pi ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.15</label>
                        <caesura/> āturaś cāpi yaṃ deśam abhīkṣṇaṃ parirakṣati | <caesura/>
                        saṃvāhyamāno bahuśas tatra śalyaṃ vinirdiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.16</label>
                        <caesura/> alpābādham aśūnaṃ ca nīrujaṃ nirupadravam | <caesura/> prasannaṃ
                        mṛduparyantaṃ nirāghaṭṭamanunnatam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.17</label>
                        <caesura/> eṣaṇyā sarvato dṛṣṭvā yathāmārgaṃ cikitsakaḥ | <caesura/>
                        prasārākuñcanān nūnaṃ niḥśalyam iti nirdiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.18</label>
                        <caesura/> asthyātmakaṃ bhajyate tu śalyamantaś ca śīryate | <caesura/>
                        prāyo nirbhujyate śārṅgam āyasaṃ ceti niścayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.19</label>
                        <caesura/> vārkṣavaiṇavatārṇāni nirhrayante tu no yadi | <caesura/> pacanti
                        raktaṃ māṃsaṃ ca kṣipram etāni dehinām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.20</label>
                        <caesura/> kānakaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ raitikaṃ trapusīsakam | <caesura/>
                        cirasthānād vilīyante pittatejaḥpratāpanāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.21</label>
                        <caesura/> svabhāvaśītā mṛdavo ye cānye 'pīdṛśā matāḥ | <caesura/>
                        dravībhūtāḥ śarīre 'sminn ekatvaṃ yānti dhātubhiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.22</label>
                        <caesura/> viṣāṇadantakeśāsthiveṇudārūpalāni tu | <caesura/> śalyāni na
                        viśīryante śarīre mṛnmayāni ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.26.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.26.23</label>
                        <caesura/> dvividhaṃ pañcagatimattvagādivraṇavastuṣu | <caesura/> viśliṣṭaṃ
                        vetti yaḥ śalyaṃ sa rājñaḥ kartum arhati || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrtasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne pranaṣṭaśalyavijñānīyo nāma
                        ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>

                <div n="27" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> saptaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaḥ śalyāpanayanīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.3</label>
                        <caesura/> śalyaṃ dvividhamavabaddhamanavabaddhaṃ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.4</label>
                        <caesura/> tatra samāsenānavabaddhaśalyoddharaṇārthaṃ pañcadaśa hetūn
                        vakṣyāmaḥ | tad yathā svabhāvaḥ pācanaṃ bhedanaṃ dāraṇaṃ pīḍanaṃ pramārjanaṃ
                        nirdhmāpanaṃ vamanaṃ virecanaṃ prakṣālanaṃ pratimarśaḥ pravāhaṇaṃ ācūṣaṇaṃ
                        ayaskānto harṣaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.5</label>
                        <caesura/> tatrāśrukṣavathūdgārakāsamūtrapurīṣānilaiḥ svabhāvabalapravṛttair
                        nayanādibhyaḥ patati māṃsāvagāḍhaṃ śalyamavidahyamānaṃ pācayitvā
                        prakothā(ā.pā)ttasya pūyaśoṇitavegād gauravād vā patati | pakvamabhidyamānaṃ
                        bhedayed dārayed vā | bhinnamanirasyamānaṃ pīḍanīyaiḥ pīḍayet pāṇibhir vā |
                        aṇūny akṣaśalyāni pariṣecanādhmāpanair bālavastrapāṇibhiḥ pramārjayet |
                        āhāraśeṣaśleṣmahīnāṇuśalyāni śvasanotkāsanapradhamanair nirdhamet |
                        annaśalyāni vamanāṅgulipratimarśaprabhṛtibhiḥ | virecanaiḥ pakvāśayagatāni |
                        vraṇadoṣāśayagatāni prakṣālanaiḥ | vātamūtrapurīṣagarbhasaṅgeṣu
                        pravāhaṇamuktaṃ | mārutodakasaviṣarudhiraduṣṭastanyeṣv ācūṣaṇam āsyena
                        viṣāṇair vā | anulomam anavabaddham akarṇam analpavraṇamukham ayaskāntena |
                        hṛdy avasthitam anekakāraṇotpannaṃ śokaśalyaṃ harṣeṇeti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.6</label>
                        <caesura/> sarvaśalyānāṃ tu mahatām aṇūnāṃ vā dvāv evāharaṇahetū bhavataḥ
                        pratilomo 'nulomaś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.7-8">

                        <caesura/> tatra pratilomamarvācīnamānayet anulomaṃ parācīnam || <label>1931
                            ed. 1.27.8</label> uttuṇḍitaṃ chitvā nirghātayecchedanīyamukham || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.9">

                        <caesura/> chedanīyamukhānyapi kukṣivakṣaḥkakṣāvaṃkṣaṇaparśukāntarapatitāni
                        ca hastaśakyaṃ yathāmārgeṇa hastenaivāpahartuṃ prayateta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.12</label>
                        <caesura/> tataḥ śalyam uddhṛtya nirlohitaṃ vraṇaṃ kṛtvā svedārham
                        agnighṛtaprabhṛtibhiḥ saṃsvedya vidahya pradihya sarpirmadhubhyāṃ
                        baddhvā+ācārikam upadiśet | (? sirāsnāyuvilagnaṃ śalākādibhir vimocyāpanayet
                        śvayathugrastavāraṅgaṃ samavapīḍya śvayathuṃ durbalavāraṅgaṃ kuśādibhir
                        baddhvā |) </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.13">

                        yathāmārgaṃ durupaharam anyato 'pabādhyamānaṃ pāṭayitvoddharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.14">

                        <caesura/> asthivivarapraviṣṭam asthividaṣṭaṃ vā'vagṛhya pādābhyāṃ
                        yantreṇāpaharet aśakyamevaṃ vā balavadbhiḥ suparigṛhītasya yantreṇa
                        grāhayitvā śalyavāraṅgaṃ pravibhujya dhanurguṇair baddhaikataś cāsya
                        pañcāṅgyām upasaṃyatasyāśvasya vaktrakavike badhnīyāt athainaṃ kaśayā
                        tāḍayed yathonnamayan śiro vegena śalyam uddharati dṛḍhāṃ vā vṛkṣaśākhām
                        avanamya tasyāṃ pūrvavad baddhvoddharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.15">

                        <caesura/> adeśottuṇḍitamaṣṭhīlāśmamudgarāṇāmnyatamasya prahāreṇa vicālya
                        yathāmārgam eva yantreṇa || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.16">

                        karṇavantyanābādhakaradeśottuṇḍitāni purastādeva || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.17">

                        <caesura/> jātuṣe kaṇṭhāsakte kaṇṭhe nāḍīṃ praveśyāgnitaptāṃ ca śalākāṃ tayā
                        'vagṛhya śītābhir adbhiḥ pariṣicya sthirībhūtām uddharet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.18-21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.27.18-21</label>
                        <caesura/> ajātuṣaṃ jatumadhūcchiṣṭapraliptayā śalākayā pūrvakalpenetyeke ||
                            <label>1931 ed. 1.27.19</label> asthiśalyamanyadvā
                        tiryakkaṇṭhāsaktamavekṣya keśoṇḍukaṃ dṛḍhaikasūtrabaddhaṃ dravabhaktopahitaṃ
                        pāyayed ākaṇṭhāt pūrṇakoṣṭhaṃ ca vāmayet vamataś ca śalyaikadeśasaktaṃ
                        jñātvā sūtraṃ sahasā tvākṣipet mṛdunā vā dantadhāvanakūrcakenāpaharet
                        praṇudedvā'ntaḥ | kṣatakaṇṭhāya ca madhusarpiṣī leḍhuṃ
                        prayacchettriphalācūrṇaṃ vā madhuśarkarāvimiśram || <label>1931 ed.
                            1.27.20</label> udakapūrṇodaramavākśirasamavapīḍayed dhunīyādvāmayed vā
                        bhasmarāśau vā nikhanedāmukhāt || <label>1931 ed. 1.27.21</label> grāsaśalye
                        tu kaṇṭhāsakte niḥśaṅkamanavabuddhaṃ skandhe muṣṭinā'bhihanyāt snehaṃ madyaṃ
                        pānīyaṃ vā pāyayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.27.22">

                        buddhimān | <caesura/> tathā yantrapṛthaktvaṃ ca samyak śalyamathāharet || </l>

                    <head> triṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaḥ pañcendriyārthavipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.3</label>
                        <caesura/> śarīraśīlayor yasya prakṛter vikṛtir bhavet | <caesura/> tat tva
                        riṣṭaṃ samāsena vyāsatas tu nibodha me || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.4</label>
                        <caesura/> śṛṇoti vividhān śabdān yo divyānām abhāvataḥ | <caesura/>
                        samudrapurameghānām asaṃpattau ca niḥsvanān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.5</label>
                        <caesura/> tān svanānnāvagṛhṇāti manyate cānyaśabdavat | <caesura/>
                        grāmyāraṇyasvanāṃś cāpi viparītān śṛṇoti ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.6</label>
                        <caesura/> dviṣacchabdeṣu ramate suhṛcchabdeṣu kupyati | <caesura/> na
                        śṛṇoti ca yo 'kasmāttaṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.7</label>
                        <caesura/> yas tūṣṇam iva gṛhṇāti śītamuṣṇaṃ ca śītavat | <caesura/>
                        saṃjātaśītapiḍako yaś ca dāhena pīḍyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.8</label>
                        <caesura/> uṣṇagātro 'timātraṃ ca yaḥ śītena pravepate | <caesura/> prahārān
                        nābhijānāti yo 'ṅgacchedamathāpi vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.9</label>
                        <caesura/> pāṃśunevāvakīrṇāni yaś ca gātrāṇi manyate | <caesura/> varṇānyatā
                        vā rājyo vā yasya gātre bhavanti hi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.10</label>
                        <caesura/> snātānuliptaṃ yaṃ cāpi bhajante nīlamakṣikāḥ | <caesura/>
                        sugandhirvā'ti yo 'kasmāt taṃ bruvanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.11</label>
                        <caesura/> viparītena gṛhṇāti rasān yaś copayojitān | <caesura/> upayuktāḥ
                        kramādyasya rasā doṣābhivṛddhaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.12</label>
                        <caesura/> yasya doṣāgnisāmyaṃ ca kuryur mithyopayojitāḥ | <caesura/> yo vā
                        rasān na saṃvetti gatāsuṃ taṃ pracakṣate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.13</label>
                        <caesura/> sugandhaṃ vetti durgandhaṃ durgandhasya sugandhitām | <caesura/>
                        gṛhṇīte vā 'nyathā gandhaṃ śānte dīpe ca nīrujaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.14</label>
                        <caesura/> yo vā gandhān na jānāti gatāsuṃ taṃ vinirdiśet | <caesura/>
                        dvandvānyuṣṇahimādīni kālāvasthā diśas tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.15</label>
                        <caesura/> viparītena gṛhṇāti bhāvān anyāṃś ca yo naraḥ | <caesura/> divā
                        jyotīṃṣi yaś cāpi jvalitānīva paśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.16</label>
                        <caesura/> rātrau sūryaṃ jvalantaṃ vā divā vā candravarcasam | <caesura/>
                        ameghopaplave yaś ca śakracāpataḍidguṇān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.17</label>
                        <caesura/> taḍittvato 'sitān yo vā nirmale gagane ghanān | <caesura/>
                        vimānayānaprāsādair yaś ca saṃkulamambaram || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.18</label>
                        <caesura/> yaś cānilaṃ mūrtimantam antarikṣaṃ ca paśyati | <caesura/>
                        dhūmanīhāravāsobhir āvṛtām iva medinīm || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.19</label>
                        <caesura/> pradīptam iva lokaṃ ca yo vā plutam ivāmbhasā | <caesura/> bhūmim
                        aṣṭāpadākārāṃ lekhābhir yaś ca paśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.20</label>
                        <caesura/> na paśyati sanakṣatrāṃ yaś cā devīm arundhatīm | <caesura/>
                        dhruvam ākāśagaṅgāṃ vā taṃ vadanti gatāyuṣam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.21</label>
                        <caesura/> jyotsnādarśoṣṇatoyeṣu chāyāṃ yaś ca na paśyati | <caesura/>
                        paśyaty ekāṅgahīnāṃ vā vikṛtāṃ vā'nyasattvajām || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.22</label>
                        <caesura/> śvakākakaṅkagṛdhrāṇāṃ pretānāṃ yakṣarakṣasām | <caesura/>
                        piśācoraganāgānāṃ bhūtānāṃ vikṛtām api || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.30.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.30.23</label>
                        <caesura/> yo vā mayūrakaṇṭhābhaṃ vidhūmaṃ vahnim īkṣate | <caesura/>
                        āturasya bhaven mṛtyuḥ svastho vyādhim āvāpnuyāt || </l>


                    <p xml:id="SS.1.30.trailer"> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        pañcendriyārthavipratipattir nāma triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>
                </div>


                <div n="31" type="adhyāya">
                    <head> ekatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ |</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.1">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.1</label>
                        <caesura/> athātaś chāyāvipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.2">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.2</label>
                        <caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.3">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.3</label>
                        <caesura/> śyāvā lohitikā nīlā pītikā vā'pi mānavam | <caesura/>
                        abhidravanti yaṃ chāyāḥ sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.4">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.4</label>
                        <caesura/> hrīr apakramate yasya prabhādhṛtismṛtiśriyaḥ | <caesura/> akasmād
                        yaṃ bhajante vā sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.5">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.5</label>
                        <caesura/> yasyādharauṣṭhaḥ patitaḥ kṣiptaś cordhvaṃ tathottaraḥ |
                        <caesura/> ubhau vā jāmbavābhāsau durlabhaṃ tasya jīvitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.6">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.6</label>
                        <caesura/> āraktā daśanā yasya śyāvā vā syuḥ patanti vā | <caesura/>
                        khañjanapratimā vā'pi taṃ gatāyuṣam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.7">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.7</label>
                        <caesura/> kṛṣṇā stabdhā'valiptā vā jihvā śūnā ca yasya vai | <caesura/>
                        karkaśā vā bhavedyasya so 'cirād vijahāty asūn || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.8">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.8</label>
                        <caesura/> kuṭilā sphuṭitā vā'pi śuṣkā vā yasya nāsikā | <caesura/>
                        avasphūrjati magnā vā na sa jīvati mānavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.9">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.9</label>
                        <caesura/> saṃkṣipte viṣame stabdhe rakte sraste ca locane | <caesura/>
                        syātāṃ vā prasrute yasya sa gatāyurnaro dhruvam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.10">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.10</label>
                        <caesura/> keśāḥ sīmantino yasya saṃkṣipte vinate bhruvau | <caesura/>
                        lunanti cākṣipakṣmāṇi so 'cirādyāti mṛtyave || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.11">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.11</label>
                        <caesura/> nāharaty annam āsyasthaṃ na dhārayati yaḥ śiraḥ | <caesura/>
                        ekāgradṛṣṭir mūḍhātmā sadyaḥ prāṇān jahāti saḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.12">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.12</label>
                        <caesura/> balavān durbalo vā'pi saṃmohaṃ yo 'dhigacchati | <caesura/>
                        utthāpyamāno bahuśastaṃ pakvaṃ bhiṣagādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.13">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.13</label>
                        <caesura/> uttānaḥ sarvadā śete pādau vikurute ca yaḥ | <caesura/>
                        viprasāraṇaśīlo vā na sa jīvati mānavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.14">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.14</label>
                        <caesura/> śītapādakarocchvāsaś chinnocchvāsaś ca yo bhavet | <caesura/>
                        kākocchvāsaś ca yo martyas taṃ dhīraḥ parivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.15">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.15</label>
                        <caesura/> nidrā na chidyate yasya yo vā jāgarti sarvadā | <caesura/> muhyed
                        vā vaktukāmaś ca pratyākhyeyaḥ sa jānatā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.16">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.16</label>
                        <caesura/> uttarauṣṭhaṃ ca yo lihyād utkārāṃś ca karoti yaḥ | <caesura/>
                        pretair vā bhāṣate sārdhaṃ pretarūpaṃ tam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.17">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.17</label>
                        <caesura/> svebhyaḥ saromakūpebhyo yasya raktaṃ pravartate | <caesura/>
                        puruṣasyāviṣārtasya sadyo jahyāt sa jīvitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.18">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.18</label>
                        <caesura/> vātāṣṭhīlā tu hṛdaye yasyor dhvam anuyāyinī | <caesura/>
                        rujā'nnavidveṣakarī sa parāsur asaṃśayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.19">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.19</label>
                        <caesura/> ananyopadravakṛtaḥ śophaḥ pādasamutthitaḥ | <caesura/> puruṣaṃ
                        hanti nārīṃ tu mukhajo guhyajo dvayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.20">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.20</label>
                        <caesura/> atisāro jvaro hikkā chardiḥ śūnāṇḍameḍhratā | <caesura/> śvāsinaḥ
                        kāsino vā'pi yasya taṃ kṣīṇam ādiśet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.21">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.21</label>
                        <caesura/> svedo dāhaś ca balavān hikkā śvāsaś ca mānavam | <caesura/>
                        balavantam api prāṇair viyuñjanti na saṃśayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.22">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.22</label>
                        <caesura/> śyāvā jihvā bhaved yasya savyaṃ cākṣi nimajjati | <caesura/>
                        mukhaṃ ca jāyate pūti yasya taṃ parivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.23">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.23</label>
                        <caesura/> vaktram āpūryate 'śrubhiḥ svidyataś caraṇāv ubhau | <caesura/>
                        cakṣuś cākulatāṃ yāti yamarāṣṭraṃ gamiṣyataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.24">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.24</label>
                        <caesura/> atimātraṃ laghūni syur gātrāṇi gurukāṇi vā | <caesura/>
                        yasyākasmāt sa vijñeyo gantā vaivasvatālayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.25">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.25</label>
                        <caesura/> paṅkamatsyavasātailaghṛtagandhāṃś ca ye narāḥ | <caesura/>
                        mṛṣṭagandhāṃś ca ye vānti gantāras te yamālayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.26">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.26</label>
                        <caesura/> yūkā lalāṭam āyānti baliṃ nāśnanti vāyasāḥ | <caesura/> yeṣāṃ
                        vā'pi ratir nāsti yātāras te yamālayam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.27">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.27</label>
                        <caesura/> jvarātisāraśophāḥ syur yasyānyonyāvasādinaḥ | <caesura/>
                        prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya nāsau śakyaś cikitsitum || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.28">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.28</label>
                        <caesura/> kṣīṇasya yasya kṣuttṛṣṇe hṛdyair miṣṭair hitais tathā |
                        <caesura/> na śāmyato 'nnapānaiś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.29">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.29</label>
                        <caesura/> pravāhikā śiraḥśūlaṃ koṣṭhaśūlaṃ ca dāruṇam | <caesura/> pipāsā
                        balahāniś ca tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.30">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.30</label>
                        <caesura/> viṣameṇopacāreṇa karmabhiś ca purākṛtaiḥ | <caesura/> anityatvāc
                        ca jantūnāṃ jīvitaṃ nidhanaṃ vrajet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.31">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.31</label>
                        <caesura/> pretā bhūtāḥ piśācāś ca rakṣāṃsi vividhāni ca | <caesura/>
                        maraṇābhimukhaṃ nityam upasarpanti mānavam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.32">
                        <label>1931 ed. 1.31.32</label>
                        <caesura/> tāni bheṣajavīryāṇi pratighnanti jighāṃsayā | <caesura/> tasmān
                        moghāḥ kriyāḥ sarvā bhavanty eva gatāyuṣām || </l>
                    <p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
                        chāyāvipratipattirnāmaikatriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ || </p>

                </div>



            </div>
